118a6(mdo sde): lta ste/ 'dod pas 'gro ba ma yin par mi 'gro ba dang / zhe sdang gis 'gre ba ma yin par mi 'gro ba dang / gti mugi ga 'gro ba ma yin mi 'gro ba dang / 'jigs/
118a7(mdo sde): pa sa 'gro ba ma yin mi 'gro ba ste/ bzhi po 'di dag go/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ting nge 'dzin gyi rgyan ni lnga po 'di dag gi/ lnga gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ sgrib
118a8(mdo sde): ba lnga spong ba'o// lnga gang zhe na 'dod par bya ba la 'dod pa dang / gnod sems dang rmugs pa dang / gnyid dang rgod pa dang / 'gyod pa the tsom ste/ sgri pa lnga po 'di dag spongs pa'o//
118a9(mdo sde): rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ting nge 'dzin gyi rgyan ni drug po 'di dag go/ drug gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa dang / chos rjes su dran pa dang / dge 'dun
118b1(mdo sde): rjes su dran pa dang / gtong ba rjes su dran pa dang / tshul khrims rjes su dran pa dang / lha rjes su dran pa ste/ drug po 'di dag go// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ting nge 'dzin gyi
118b2(mdo sde): rgyan ni bdun po 'di dag go/ bdun gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa'i mi rjed pa'i byang chub kyi yan lag bdun bsgom ste/ dran pa yang dag byang chub kyi yan lag dang / chos
118b3(mdo sde): rab tu 'byed pa yang dag byang chub yan lag dang / brtson 'grus yang dag byang chub kyi yan lag dang / shin tu sbyangs pa yang dag byang chub kyi yan lag dang / ting nge 'dzin yang dag byang
118b4(mdo sde): chub kyi yan lag dang / btang snyoms yang dag byang chub kyi yan lag dang / bdun po 'di dag go// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ting nge 'dzin gyi rgyan ni brgyad po 'di dag go//
118b5(mdo sde): brgyad gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad po sgom pa ste/ 'di ltar yang dag par lta ba dang / yang dag par rtog pa dang / yang dag pa'i ngag dang / yang dag pa
118b6(mdo sde): las kyi mtha' dang / yang dag pa'i mcho ba dang / yang dag pa'i rtsol ba dang / yang dag pa'i dran pa dang / yang dag pa'i ting nge 'dzin te brgyad po 'di dag go// rigs kyi bu byang chub sen
118b7(mdo sde): dpa' rnams kyi ting nge 'dzin gyi rgyan ni dgu po 'di dag go// dgu gang zhe na rigs kyi bu 'di la byang chub sems dpa' brjed pa med pa'i sems kyi snying rje chen po'i gnas la gnas te/
118b8(mdo sde): sems can thams cad yongs su mi gtong bar gnas nas/ 'dod pa rnams la dben pa sdig pa mi dge ba'i chos rnams las dben pa/ rnam par rtog pa bcas pa/ rnam par spyod pa/
119a1(mdo sde): dang bcas pa dben pa las skyes pa'i dga' ba dang / bde ba can bsam gtan dang po rdzogs par byas te gnas so// de rnam par rtog pa dang / rnam par spyod pa
119a2(mdo sde): nye bar zhi ba ste nang shin tu dang zhing sems kyi rgyud gcig tu gyur pas/ rnam par rtog pa med cing / rnam par spyod pa med pa/ ting nge 'dzin las skyes pa dga' ba dang bde ba can/ bsam
119a3(mdo sde): gtan gnyis pa rdzogs par byas te gnas so// dga' ba'i 'dod chags dang bral te/ btang snyoms can du gnas pa la dran pa dang / ldan zhing bshes bzhin gyis bde ba la lus kyi tshor te/
119a4(mdo sde): gang 'phags pa rnams kyis btang snyoms can du dran pa dang ldan zhing bde bar gnas pa'o zhes brjod pa dga' ba med pa'i bsam gtan gsum pa rdzogs par byas te gnas so// de bde
119a5(mdo sde): ba yang spangs sdug bsngal ba yang spangs te bde ba dang / yid mi bde ba snga nas nub pas/ bde ba yang med sdug bsngal ba yang med de btang snyoms dang dran pas yongs su dag pa
119a6(mdo sde): bsam gtan bzhi pa rdzogs par bas te gnas so// de rnam pa thams cad du gzugs kyis 'du shes las shin tu 'das te/ thogs pa'i 'du shes rnams kyi rgyan ni gnyis po 'di byed pa// /
119a7(mdo sde): namakha' mtha' yas so snyam nas/ nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched rdzogs par byas te gnas so// de rnam pa thams cad du na mkha' mtha' yas skye mched las shin tu 'das te/ rnam
119a8(mdo sde): par shes pa mtha' yas so snyam nas/ rnam shes mtha' yos skye mched las 'das par byas ste gnas so// de rnam pa thams cad du rnam shes mtho' yas skye mched las shin tu 'das te/
119b1(mdo sde): cing yang med do snyam nas ci yang med pa'i skye mched rdzogs par byas te gnas so// de rnam pa thams cad du ci'ang med pa'i skye mched las shin tu 'das te/ 'di shin med min skye mched rdzogs
119b2(mdo sde): par byas te gnas so// de rnam pa thams cad 'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched las 'das te/ 'du sheso dang tshor ba dang 'gog pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa la/ snyoms par
119b3(mdo sde): 'jug kyang / thabs mkhas pas yang dag pa'i mtha' mngon sum du 'ong mi byed la/ sngon gyi byin brlabs kyis yang langs nas/ sems can rnams kyang yongs su smin par byed pa ste/
119b4(mdo sde): ting nge 'dzin gyi rgyan ni chu bo 'di dag go// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ting nge 'dzin gyi rgyan ni bcu po 'di dag gi/ bcu gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ mi khrug pas nges par nges
119b5(mdo sde): bor sems pa dang / zhi gnas dngos su rdzogs par byed pa dang / mngon par brtson pa mi 'dor ba dang / nang du yang dag 'jogs sred pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams chud mi za ba dang /
119b6(mdo sde): sems dben pa dang / lus shin tu spungs pa dang / chos rnams la sems shing 'jal la so sor rtogs pa dang / sems la dbang sgyur ba dang / 'phags pa'i rigs rab tu thob pa
119b7(mdo sde): ste/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ting nge 'dzin gyi rgyan ni bcu po 'di dag go/ rigs kyi bu de la byang chub sems dpa'i rnams kyi shes rab kyi rgyan gang zhe na/ rigs kyi bu
119b8(mdo sde): byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi shes rab kyi rgyan ni gcig go// gcig gang zhe na 'di lta ste chos thams cad la the tshom med pa ste/ 'di gcig go// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpal
120a1(mdo sde): smra stsa du gas sa
120a2(mdo sde): kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi shes rab kyi rgyan ni gsum po 'di dag go/ gsum gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ gti mug spong ba dang / ma rigs pa'i sgo nga'i sbubs nges
120a3(mdo sde): bar gcog pa dang / mun pa mun nag sel ba sel ba ste/ gsum po 'di dag go/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi shes rab kyi rgyan ni bzhi po 'di dag go/ bzhi gang
120a4(mdo sde): zhe na 'di lta ste/ sdug bsngal yongs su shes par bya ba'i shes pa dang / kun tu 'byung ba spong ba'i snang ba dang / 'gog pa mngon gsum du bya ba'i 'od dang / lam sgom pa'i byin
120a5(mdo sde): brlabs te bzhi po 'di dag go/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi shes rab kyi rgyan ni 'di dag go// lnga gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ dmigs pa med pas tshul khrims kyi phung
120a6(mdo sde): po yongs su dag pa dang / shes rab mchog gi bsam gtan pa yin pas/ ting nge 'dzin gyi phung po yongs su dag pa dang / gnyis dang bral bas rnam par grol ba'i phung po yongs su
120a7(mdo sde): dag pa dang / dus gsum mnyam pa nyid pas rnam par grol bar ye shes mthong ba'i phung po yongs su dag pa ste/ 'dod chags bral ba'i chos nyid pas chos kyi phung po yongs su
120a8(mdo sde): dag pa ste/ lnga po 'di dag go/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi shes rab kyi rgyan ni drug po 'di dag go// drug gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ 'khor gsum yongs su dag
120b1(mdo sde): kha'i sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa ni/ sgyu ma dang mnyam pa nyid pas bdag gi 'khor yongs su dag pa ste/ mi lam dang mnyam pa nyid pas/ sems can gyi 'khor yongs su dag pa dang /
120b2(mdo sde): rnam par smin pa la re ba med pas byang chub kyi 'khor yongs su dag po// 'khor gsum yongs su dag pa'i tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni/ gzugs rnyan lta bu'i phyir lus kyi
120b3(mdo sde): 'khor yongs su dag pa dang / lta bu'i shes pa gang ga'i 'khor yongs su dag pa dag dang / sgyu ma dang mnyam pa nyid pas sems kyi 'khor yongs su dag pa'o// 'khor
120b4(mdo sde): gsum yongs su dag pa'i bzod pa'i bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa ni nyes par smras pa'i tshig rnams la khro khro ba spong ba yongs su dag pa'o// bstod pa dang sngags pa dang / rjes
120b5(mdo sde): su 'chags pa yongs su dag pa dang / yan lag dang nyin lag gcod pa dag la chos kyi ska la rab tu rtog pa yongs su dag pa'o// 'khor gsum yongs su dag pa'i brtson 'grus kyi pha rol
120b6(mdo sde): tu phyin pa ni 'khor ba rmi lam lta bur mos pas yongs su mi skyo ba yongs su dag pa dang / rdo rje lta bu'i bsam gtan yongasu dag pa dang / mtshan ma thams cad las grol bas blang ba med dang /
120b7(mdo sde): dor ba med pa yongs su dag pa'o// 'khor gsum yongs su dag pa'i bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni 'gyur shes pas de la ma chags pa yongs su dag pa dang / mngon par shes
120b8(mdo sde): pa med pas/ lhag mthong yongs su dag pa dang / mngon par shes pa skyed pa'i dmigs pas yongs su dag pa'o// 'khor gsum yongs su dag pa'i thabs kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni//
121a1(mdo sde): sems can yongs su smin par byed pas/ bsdu ba'i dngos po yongs su dag pa dang / dam pa'i chos yongs su 'dzin pas gzungs yong su dag pa dang / sangs/
121a2(mdo sde): rgyas kyi zhing gi rgyan gyi phyir smon lam yongs su dag pa ste/ drug po 'di dag go/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rgyan ni bdun po 'di dag go/ bdun gang zhe na 'di lta ste/
121a3(mdo sde): dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams la dran pa med cing / yid la byed pa med pa dang / yang dag par sreng ba rnams la skye ba med pa dang / 'gag pa med par shes pa dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams
121a4(mdo sde): kyis lus dang sems dben pa dang / dbang po rnams la dbang po yongasu shes pa dang / stobs rnams kyis bdud nyon mongs pa thams cad tshar gcod pa dang / byang chub kyi yan lag rnams
121a5(mdo sde): kyi chos thams cad kyi ngo bo nyid dang lam rnams la 'ong ba med pa dang / 'gro ba med par shes pa ste/ dngos po 'di dag go/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi shes rab
121a6(mdo sde): kyi rgyan ni brgyad po 'di dag go/ brgyad gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ shin tu zhi ba'i phyir zhi gnas shis pa dang / rab rib dang bral ba'i phyir lhag mthong shes pa dang / chos kyi phung po rjes
121a7(mdo sde): rtogs pa'i phyir phung po shes pa dang / na mkha'i khams dang mnyam pa nyid kyi phyir skye mched shes pa dang / bdag med pa'i phyir rton cing 'brel par 'byung ba shes pa dang / mi khrugs
121a8(mdo sde): pa'i phyir bden pa shes pa dang / yang dag pa ji lta bu bzhin du rab tu rtogs pas chos thams cad nges par rtogs pa shes pa ste/ brgyad po 'di dge go/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sem
121b1(mdo sde): dpa' rnams kyi shes rab kyi rgya ni dgu po 'di dag go/ dgu gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ sngon gyi mtha' dag 'das pa dang shes pa dang / phyi mi'i mtha' dag ma 'ongs pa shes pa dang / bar
121b2(mdo sde): gyi mtha' dag da ltar byung ba shes pa dang / rgyu chud mi za bas nges pa rnams sar shes dang / rkyen nye bar bsgrubs pas nges pa rnams shes pa dang / yongs su smin par byed pas/
121b3(mdo sde): logs pa nyid du nges pa rnams nges pa dang / chos kyi sku rab tu phye ba'i phyir/ sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam pa nyid du shes pa dang / 'dod chags dang bral ba'i chos kyi phyir chos thams
121b4(mdo sde): cad mnyam pa nyid du shes pa dang / 'dus ma byas kyis rab tu phye ba'i phyir/ 'phags pa thams cad mnyam pa nyid du shes pa ste/ dgu po 'di dag go// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems
121b5(mdo sde): dpa' rnams kyi shes rab kyi rgyan ni bcu po 'di dgo/ bcu gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ rnam par bsgrub pa mtshan nyid kyi phyir sgyu ma lta bur shes pa dang / yongs su brtags pa'i mtshan
121b6(mdo sde): nyid kyis phyir rmi lam lta bur shes pa dang / rnam par 'khrul pa'i mtshan nyid kyi phyir smig rgyu lta bur shes pa dang / 'pho ba med pa'i mtshan nyid kyi phyir gzugs rnyan lta bur shes
121b7(mdo sde): ba dang / 'du 'phrod kyi mtshan nyid phyir mig yor lta bur shes pa dang / rkyen gyi mtshan nyid kyi phyir brag cha lta bur shes pa dang / chos kyi dbyings 'dres pa med pa'i mtshan nyid du shes
121b8(mdo sde): ba dang / de bzhin nyid gnas pa med pa'i mtshan du shes pa dang / yang dag pa'i mtha' mi 'khrug pa'i mtshan nyid du shes pa dang / 'das byas dag 'dus byas kyi sa mtshan nyid/
122a1(mdo sde): @du shes pa ste/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi shes rab kyi rgyan ni bcu po 'di dag go/ rigs kyi bu de la byang chub sems dpa' rnams
122a2(mdo sde): gzungs kyi rgyan gang zhe na/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams gzungs kyi rgyan ni gcig go/ gcig gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ dran par byed pa med pa ste/ 'di ni gcig go// /

122a5(mdo sde): ba ste/ gsum po 'di dag go/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi gzungs kyi rgyan ni bzhi po 'di dag go/ bzhi gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ chags pa med pa'i tshigs dang / rtsa ba
122a6(mdo sde): ba ma yin pa'i tshigs dang / brdzun med pa'i tshig ste bzhi po 'di dag gi// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rgyan ni lnga po 'di dag go/ gang lnga gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ thos pa
122a7(mdo sde): thams cad kyi nang nas don la rtog pa dang / yi ge'i tshogs thams cad kyi nang nas ye shes la rten pa dang / mdo sde thams cad kyi nang nas nges pa'i don gyi mdo sde la ston pa dang / gang zagi smra
122a8(mdo sde): thams lnga chos nyid ston pa dang / 'jig rten thams cad la 'jig rten las 'das pa la rton pa ste/ lnga po 'di dag go// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rgyan ni drug po 'di dado//
122b1(mdo sde): drug gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ ji skad smras pa de bzhin du byed pa dang / dben pa'i rjes su 'thun pa'i tshig rab tu thob pa dang / nga rgyal med pas gzungs par 'os pa'i tshig dang g.yo med pas
122b2(mdo sde): blang bar 'os pa'i tshig dang / snying rje chen po sbyor bas 'bras bu yod pa'i chos ston pa dang / snod la mkhas pas khyad par chos ston pa dang / 'jig rten shes pas dus su chos ston pa ste/

122b4(mdo sde): can gyi spobs pa dang / myur ba'i spobs pa dang / chags pa med pa'i spobs pa dang / rgyun chad pa med pa'i spobs pa dang / 'khrul pa med pa'i spobs pa dang / shin tu nges
122b5(mdo sde): pa'i tshigs gis spobs pa ste/ bdun po 'di dag go// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi gzungs kyi rgyan ni brgyad po 'di dag go/ brgyad gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ lha'i skad

124a1(mdo sde): / dang 'dri ba rnams la nges par 'byung ba shes pa dang / mngon pa'i nga rgyal can rnams la snrel zhi bstan pa shes pa dang / yang dag par zhugs/

124a8(mdo sde): gis mchog dam pa 'di mdzes so// blo gros rnams kyi rgyad bzhi ste// tshul khrims ting 'dzin de bzhin shes rab mchog/ shin tu rnams nges don dang de bzhin gzungs// de ni lus
124b1(mdo sde): ca kun gyis yid 'ong dga'// lus dang ngag rnams dang ni yang dag cing // de'i rnam par ltung ba kun chad pa// 'di ni tshul khrims ldan pa'i rgyun yin na// lha mi rnams kyi nang du me khas pa
124b2(mdo sde): skye// de'i smon lam ji ltar 'dod pa bzhin du 'grub// nan tan snying por bla dang yang ldan// 'di ni tshul khrims dag pa'i rgyan yin no// de'i ting nge 'dzin sgyu ma ma yin te// shes
124b3(mdo sde): rab rnam grol de bzhin ye shes mthong // de'i mya ngan 'das pa sgyu ma min// 'di ni tshul khrims rnam par dag pa'i rgyan// tshul khrims skyon med tshul khrims rnam par dag/ tshul
124b4(mdo sde): khrims 'thun chags ma yin 'dren med// de'i rangs dga' de bzhengs rarangs dbang yin// 'di ni tshul khrims pang dag pa'i rgyan// tshul khrims kyis ni sbyin pa dag par 'gyur/
124b5(mdo sde): bzod pa dag cing de bzhin brtson 'grus dag/ bsam gtan dag cing de bzhin shes rab dag/ thabs dang de bzhin bag yod dag yin// g.yo ba med cing brtan la shin du gnas// /
124b6(mdo sde): sa mchog thob cing rnal 'byor rnam 'phro med// lhod pa spangs shing dgang sla gso yang sla// 'di ni gang dag tshul khrims dag pa'i rgyan// brtson 'grus 'bar zhing tshul khrims
124b7(mdo sde): bsngags pa ste// de'i sems ni nam yang gdung mi 'gyur// de la yid la gcags par 'gyur med de// 'di ni gang dag tshul khrims dag pa'i rgyan// 'jigs pa med cing mi skra
124b8(mdo sde): mi zhum ste// bsam pa nges shing zhi la yid rab zhi// 'dir ni de'i bcings pa lhod par 'gyur// 'di ni gang dag tshul khrims dag pa'i rgyan// grags chen sems ni las su rung
125a1(mdo sde): ba yin// de ni dul zhing de bzhin cing shes yin// 'dir ni rang lus mtshan gyi brgyan byed pa// 'di ni gang dag tshul khrims dag pa'i rgyan// de ni ji skad smras
125a2(mdo sde): pa de bzhin byed// mkhas pa de ni ngag gi rgyan thob ste/ de ni nyon mongs pa med pas rtags sems rgyan// 'di ni gang dag tshul khrims dag pa'i rgyan// khyed par 'phags pa'i
125a3(mdo sde): zhing ni legs par rgyan// theg pa mchog la sems can yongs smin byed// gang phyin sdig thams cad mi byed pas// rang gi skye ba legs par brgyan par byed// byang chub spyod pa rtag

125a6(mdo sde): lnga po rnam par sel// bag yod gyur nas rjes su dran drug bsgom// byang chub yan lag bdun dang lam bsgom ste// mthar gyi sa dgu dang ting 'dzin bsam gtan byed// rnal 'byor
125a7(mdo sde): ba ni gzhi gnas nges sems sbyor// de ni tshul bzhin dge ba rlud mi bzod// dben dang shin tu sbyangs dang so sor rtog/ 'phags pa'i rigs la dbang ni sbyar ba yin// chos
125a8(mdo sde): rnams ni the tsom med par 'gyur// de la kun nas ldang dang 'gyur ba med// de la ma rig gti mug mun pa med// bden pa snang zhing yongs su shes pa shes// tshul khrims dag
125b1(mdo sde): pa dmigs pa med pa ste// shes rab dam pa bsam gtan ting 'dzin dag/ gnyis bsal nas ni rnam par dgrol ba dgalhag pa'i nga rgyal med cing shes pa dang // dus
125b2(mdo sde): sum dag la ye shes mthong mi chags// 'dod chags bral ba'i shes pas chos kyang dag/ dag nas 'dir ni de la rloms sems med// 'di ni shang dag shes rab ldan pa'i rgyan//
125b3(mdo sde): shes rab kyis ni sbyin pa rgyan gyur te// rmi lam sgyu ma tshol ba med pa'i phyir// bdag dang byang chub de bzhin sems rnams// 'khor gsum de dag de ni rnam par sbyong // /
125b4(mdo sde): shes rab kyi ni tshul khrims brgyan gyur te// gzugs brnyan sgyu ma brag cha 'dra ba'i phyir/ lus dang ngag rnams dang ni de bzhin sems// 'khor gsum po dag de ni rnam
125b5(mdo sde): bar spong // shes rab kyis ni bzod pa'i rgyan gyur te// khams dang mtho ba ma yin dma' bar 'gyur min dang // dam pa'i chos kun rtag tu rab rtog pa// 'khor gsum po
125b6(mdo sde): dag de ni rnam par spong // shes rab kyis ni rtson 'grus rgyan gyur te// sko ba med cing bsam gtan pa dang // de ni blang ba med cing der med pa// 'khor gsum po dag
125b7(mdo sde): de ni rnam par dag spyod// shes rab kyis ni bsam gtan rgyan gyur te// de ma chags gyur dang lhag mthong dang // mkhas pa mngon par shes pa skyed pa dang // 'khor ga suM
125b8(mdo sde): po dag de ni rnam par sbyong // shes rab kyis ni thabs dang rgyan byed de// shin tu sdu ba gzugs dang yang dag smon// 'khor gsum po dag de ni rnam par sbyong zhing // sems
127a1(mdo sde): can chos dang de bzhin zhing rnams sbyong // dran pa nye bar bzhag la dran mi 'jug/ yang dag bong ba la gnyis med de// rdzu 'phrul gyis ni lus dang sems
127a2(mdo sde): kyang dben// sems can gyis ni dbang po kun mi shes// bdud dang nyon mongs rnams kyis zil mi non// chos kyi rang bzhin tshul bzhin rjes su rtogs// de bzhin lam la 'ong med 'gro
127a3(mdo sde): ba med// 'di ni gang dag shes rab ldan pa'i rgyan// de ni shin tu zhi ba sa gzhi gnas shes pa// de'i lhag mthong spyod yul mtha' yas te// chos kyi phung po shes pa phung po bzhin// /
127a4(mdo sde): khams ni nam mkha' mtshungs shing 'dra bar shes// des ni stong pa lta bur skye mched shes// rten pas bsags pas chos rnams bdag med de// don dam dben par 'khrug pa
127a5(mdo sde): shes// tshul bzhin gyis ni nges par rtog par shes// dus gsum la ni tshogs med 'jug/ rnam par gzhag phyir phung po gsum yang shes// dkon mchog gsum ni mtshan
127a6(mdo sde): nyid gcig tu shes// 'di ni gang dag shes rab ldan pa'i rgyan// rnam sgrub mtshan nyid sgyu ma lta bur shes// yongs brtags rtsa ba rmi lam ji bzhin no// rnam 'khrul mtshan nyid smig
127a7(mdo sde): rgyu 'dra ba ste// 'pho med chos rnams gzugs rnyen mtshan nyid do// 'du 'phro byung ba mig yer lta bu ste// rkyen rnams kyis na brag cha ji bzhin no// chos kyi dbyings ni rtag tu ma 'dres shes/
127a8(mdo sde): de bzhin nyid ni gnas med de rab shes// yang dag mtha' ni rtag tu mi g.yo chos// 'dus ma byas dang 'dus byas gnyis su med// shes rab zab cing blo ni rab yangs pa/ brgyad
127b1(mdo sde): nas sangs rgyas chos rnams tshol bar byed// de ni nam yang dran pa brjed pa med// chos rnams kun tu 'dzin cing 'dzin par byed// don dang tshig 'bru la ni rtag tu mkhas//
127b2(mdo sde): nges tshigs shes pa rtag par rtogs khong chud// chags med tshig dang rtsa ba ma yin dang // rab tu grol ba'i tshig dang brdzun med tshig/ chos pa kun don rtag tu rtog pa dang //
127b3(mdo sde): mkhas pas de ni ye shes rton par byas// nges don mdo sde rtog par rab tu shes// gang zag med pa'i chos nyid rton byed cing // 'jig rten 'das pa'i chos nyid la yang brton// de
127b4(mdo sde): ni gzungs kyis brgyan par gyur pa yin// de'i tshig ni bden pa'i rjes su mthun// gzungs par 'os dang dus su 'ongs pa yin// de'i chos bstan de ni 'bras bu yod// chad pa dang
127b5(mdo sde): ni dus su rgyun chags 'jug/ de'i spobs pa mgyogs pa skye ba ste// shugs can dang ni mir dang rtag mi chags// rgyun chad med dang 'khrul med nges pa'i tshigs// nges par gyur
127b6(mdo sde): ba'i 'breng bas legs brgyan zhing // lha dang klu'i skad ni rab tu shes// gnod sprin dag dang dri za lha ma yin// mkha'i lding lha 'am ci dang lto 'phye che// sems can kun
127b7(mdo sde): byi skad dang rab tu shes// 'khor lhags shes nas spa gong med pa ste// smra ba mthong nas zhum par 'gyur ba med// 'jigs pa med par chos kyi gtam yang brjod//
127b8(mdo sde): ba rnams la nges 'byung rab tu shes// lhag pa'i nga rgyal can mthong snal gzhi'i// gtam rjod rnal 'byor mthong nas rjes su mthun// nga rgyal can la lag na rdo rje ston//
128a1(mdo sde): yul mchog chags la sred pa'i skal ba ste// thegs pa gsum gyi rim pa'i gtam yang brjod// dog pa kun gyi the tsom gcod pa ste// blo'i chos rnams
128a2(mdo sde): mngon gsum 'gyur ba yin// de'i shes rab nam yang gzhan mi ldog/ yi ge thams cad rtag tu zad med shes// don rnams nges pa dag la rgyun chad med// de ni sangs rgyas
128a3(mdo sde): chos rnams mtha' yas brjod// de ni gzungs kyis brgyan par 'gyur ba yin// kun nas nyon mongs skyon ni mtha' yas shes// rnam par byung ba'i phan yon thub pa med//
128a4(mdo sde): de bzhin sems can dbang po thams cad shes// sangs rgyas gnang ba'i so sor rig pa thob// de ni gzungs kyis brgyan par 'gyur ba ste// de'i yon tan 'di dag gzhan
128a5(mdo sde): dag kyang // skal pa rgyun chad med par rab brjod kyang // yon tan mtha' ni rtogs par mi nuso// 'phags pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying rje chen po bstan pa// /
128a6(mdo sde): bam po gsum pa / bcom ldan 'das kyis gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' gzungs kyi dbang phyug gi rgyal po bka' stsal
128a7(mdo sde): pa/ rigs kyi bu snang ba gang gis snang bar 'gyur na/ byang chub sems dpa'i mun pa mun nag dang bral zhing byang chub sems dpa' spyod pa yongs su dag spyod par 'gyur ba dang /
128a8(mdo sde): byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi snang ba ni brgyad po 'di dag go// brgyad gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ dran pa'i snang ba dang / blo gros kyi snang ba dang / rtogs pa'i snang ba dang / chos kyi snang ba dang /
128b1(mdo sde): shes pa'i snang ba dang / mngon par shes pa'i snang ba dang sgrub pa'i snang ba ste// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi snang ba ni brgyad po 'di dag go// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems
128b2(mdo sde): dpa' rnams kyi dran pa'i snang ba gang zhe na// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dran pa snang ba ni brgyad po 'di dag go// brgyad gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ sngon byas pa'i dge ba'i rtsa

128b4(mdo sde): pa dang / mi dge ba'i chos spong zhing / dge ba'i chos yongs su rdzogs par bya ba'i phyir dran pa rgya chen po phun sum tshogs par 'gyur ba dang / de dran pa phun sum tshogs par rig nas/

128b7(mdo sde): yin gyi tshig 'bru'i blo gros ma yin pa dang / ye shes kyi blo gros kyi yin gyi rnam par shes pa'i blo gros ma yin pa dang / chos kyi blo gros yin gyi/ nyon mongs pa'i blo gros ma yin pa dang /
128b8(mdo sde): rigs pa'i blo gros yin gyi// 'gyel ba'i blo gros ma yin pa dang / byang chub kyi sems kyi blo gros yin gyi/ nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi blo gros ma yin pa dang / rlabs po che'i
129a1(mdo sde): blo gros yin gyi/ chung ngu'i blo gros ma yin pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi blo gros yin gyi/ bdud kyi blo gros ma yin pa dang / snying rje chen po'i blo gros yin gyi/ sems
129a2(mdo sde): can rnam par 'tshe ba'i blo gros ma yin pa ste/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi blo gros kyi snang ba ni brgyad po 'di dag go// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi snang ba
129a3(mdo sde): ni brgyad po 'di dag go// brgyad gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ chos thams cad rtogs par khong du chud par 'gyur ba dang / dgongs te ston pa rnams rtogs par khong du chud par 'gyur ba dang /
129a4(mdo sde): sems can gyi bsam pa rnams rtogs par khong du chud par 'gyur ba dang / so so yang dag pa rig pa'i shes pa dang / ni rtogs par khong du chud par 'gyur ba dang / rten cing 'brel par
129a5(mdo sde): 'byung ba za mi rtogs par khong du chud par 'gyur ba dang / snrel zhi rgyud bstan pa rtogs par khong du chud par 'gyur ba dang / spri'u tshugs kyi rgyud bstan pa rtogs par khong du chud par
129a6(mdo sde): 'gyur ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad rtogs par khong du chud par 'gyur ba ste/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rtogs pa'i snang ba na brgyad po 'di dag go ka ri
129a7(mdo sde): kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi chos kyi snang ba ni brgyad po 'di dag go// brgyad gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ sems can rnams la las kyi bya ba la 'jug pa ston pas 'jig rten pa'i
129a8(mdo sde): chos kyi snang ba dang / thar pa 'dod pa rnams la shes rab kyi ston pa 'jig rten las 'das pa'i chos kyi sdang ba dang / lam shin tu bsgoms pa'i phyir sgrib pa med pa'i chos kyi sna
129b1(mdo sde): ba dang / 'dod pa dang srid pa dang / ma rig pa dang lta ba'i zag pa ma slob pa'i phyir zag pa med pa'i chos kyi snang ba dang / 'phags pa rnams kyi skyon pa mngon sum du byed pa'i phyir
129b2(mdo sde): 'dus ma byas kyi chos kyi snang ba dang / glo bur gyi nyon mongs pa la shin tu rtogs pa'i phyir kun nas nyon mongs pa'i chos kyi snang ba dang / sems rang bzhin gyis 'od gsal
129b3(mdo sde): ba'i phyir rnam par byang ba chos kyi snang ba dang / chos rnams shin tu nye bar zhi ba'i phyir ma ngan las 'das pa'i chos kyi snang ba ste/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi
129b4(mdo sde): snang ba ni brgyad po 'di dag go// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi shes pa'i snang ba ni brgyad po 'di dag gi/ brgyad gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ brgyad po'i shes pa'i

129b8(mdo sde): ste/ bden pa sgom pa gang gis skyon med pa 'jug pa de la de'i snang ba dang / bden pa sgom pa gags 'bras bu dang po thob par 'gyur ba de la de'i snang ba dang / bden pa bsgom pa
130a1(mdo sde): gang gis 'bras bu gnyis pa thob par 'gyur ba de la de'i snang ba dang / bden pa bsgom pa gang gis 'bras bu gsum po 'thob par 'gyur ba de la de'i snang

130b1(mdo sde): can thams cad dog sa pa'i phyir ye shes kyi tshogs kyi snang ba ste/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi mngon par shes pa'i snang bas ni brgyad po 'di dag go// rigs
130b2(mdo sde): kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sgrub pa'i snang ba ni dgu po 'di dag go/ dgu gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ sgrub pas ye shes kyi sdang ba dang / sgrub pas shes rab kyi snang

130b5(mdo sde): byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sgrub pa'i snang ba ni dgu po 'di dag go// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag gsungs so// dran pa de dang
130b6(mdo sde): yang dag 'dres pas na// sngon chad las dge stsags pa chung mi gzon// phra bar song ba phun sum 'tshogs pa de// phyi phyir zhing ni yang dag sgrub par byed// thos pa'i chos
130b7(mdo sde): rnams la ni brjed pa med pa/ rnam par gdon mi za bar myur du 'thob// nye bar zhi bas yul rnams las ni sras// dran dang ldan pa'i mi dge rnams dang bral// dran pa rgya chen po ni shin/
130b8(mdo sde): tu bstsags// bye ba bya ba dag nin par 'byed// dran pa dag dang ldan pa rig nas ni// rgyal ba rang 'byung dag gis byin gyis rlob// dam pa'i chos kyi grong khyer skyong byed pa//
131a1(mdo sde): de ni 'gro ba rnams la chos ston nus// shes rab med par mun pa rnam bral ste/ lnga dang mi rnams kyi ni don kyang byed// blo gros snang ba bzang ldan thob rgya
131a2(mdo sde): nas// dogs pa dang ni the tsom rnams kyang gcod// dran dang ldan pa rang 'byung ye shes kyis// byang chub myur tu rjes su rdzogs par byed// de ni don gyi blo gros can yin
131a3(mdo sde): gyi// tshig 'bru'i rjes su mi rgyug sgra la'ang min// sems can dag la ye shes blo gros can// rnam par shes pa'i blo gros 'dod pa ma yin pa// chos kyi blo gros ldan
131a4(mdo sde): par gyur pa de// nyon mongs blo gros sel cing gti mug bral// shes rab dang ni thabs kyi tshul shes pa// de ni rgyal ba'i byang chub 'gal med byed// de ni sangs rgyas
131a5(mdo sde): 'gyur ba'i blo gros ldan// nyan thos 'gyur min rang rgyal 'gyur ma yin// rtag tu rlabs chen blo gros can yin gyi// de ni blo gros chung ngu 'dod ma yin// sangs rgyas blo gros

131a7(mdo sde): pa gang yin de la ni// the tsom med par rtogs par khong du chud// de ni nongs te gzungs la mkhas 'gyur zhing // sems can spyod pa rnams la rtogs dang ldan// so sor
131a8(mdo sde): yang dag rig la rtog ldan ning // de'i shes pa 'jug pa chags pa med// rkyen 'byung byed pa po dang rnam bral bar// rten pa'i chos rnams dag ni rab tu shes// de ni snrel bzhir
131b1(mdo sde): rgyud la mkhas gyur cing // spyi'u tshugs ni rtogs par khong du chud// sangs rgyas kyi ni chos rnams ji snyed pa// thams cad kyang ni chos rnams ji snyed pa// thams cad kyang
131b2(mdo sde): ni rtog par khong du nud// 'jig rten pa'i chos kyi snang ba yis// lha mi rnams kyi las kyi bya ba shes// 'jig rten las ni 'das pa'i ye shes kyis// shes rab snang
131b3(mdo sde): pa'i dang ni ldan pa yin// kha na ma thor bcas dang the tsom med// ye shes rab tu gsal ba chen po 'jug/ lami na shin tu bsgoms par 'gyur ba'i phyir// rtags
131b4(mdo sde): tu 'bras bu yod pa'i chos ston to// zag par bcas dang zag pa med pa'i// chos la de ni snang ba rab tu 'jug/ de ni zag pa thams cad pang byed cing // lha dang mi rnams kyi ni
131b5(mdo sde): dod kyang byed// 'dus ma byas kyang 'dus byas chos rnams la// de'i shes pa rtag tu rab tu 'jug/ de ni de yang dri bral rab rib med// skyon med thob nas spyad pa rnams
131b6(mdo sde): kyang spyod// rnam par byang dang kun nas nyon mongs med// dri'i shes pa sgri ba med pa 'jug/ rang bzhin gyis ni sems 'od gsal ba dang // kun nas nyon mongs pa'i
131b7(mdo sde): tshul yang shes// ji ltar mya ngan 'das par gyur pa ni// skye ba med cing 'byung ba med par shes// 'di 'dra 'di ni theg pa chen po la// chos kyi snang ba mtha' yas gyur pa yin//
131b8(mdo sde): de ni brgyad pa'i ni shes pa dang / rgyun tu zhugs la shes po 'jug pa dang // lan cig phyir 'ongs pa'i shes pa dang // phyir mi 'ong la shes pa 'jug pa dang // de ni dang
132a1(mdo sde): bcom pa dang dang rgyal dang // 'jig rten 'gon po byang chub sems dpa' dag/ kun la de'i shes dang sgrub pa rnams// lhag ma lus pa med par rab tu
132a2(mdo sde): 'jug/ gang gis 'bras bu thob par 'gyur ba dang // 'khrugs med don dam nges par 'byung bar 'gyur ba// de nga rab bsgoms smra ba dpa' bo rnams// bden pa'i sdang ba
132a3(mdo sde): dag dang ldan pa yin// bden pa dag ni sgom pa byas pas na// skyon med 'jug dang 'bras bu dang po 'thob// gnyis dang gsum de bzhin bzhin pa dang // rang rgyal rnams ni 'bras
132a4(mdo sde): bu 'thob par 'gyur// sgom pa gang g+hi sa ni smra ba'i rtags// de dag bzod pa dag ni bsgom 'gyur dang // gang gis rgyal ba'i byang chub 'tshang rgya ba// bden pa de dag ni snang bar 'gyur//

132a6(mdo sde): pa'i snang ba'i sa// skal pa khrag khrig dag ni rjes su dran// 'od gsal ba'i snang ba yis// gzhan gyis sems kyi spyod pa rnams la mkhas// rdzu 'phrul gyis ni shes pa'i snang ba yin// /
132a7(mdo sde): phyogs cu'i zhing ni khrag khrig rnams su 'gro/ zag pa med pa'i shes pa'i snang ba ni// nam mkha' dang ni mtshungs shing 'dra ba yin// bsod nams kyi ni snang ba mtha' yas pa'i// mngon shes
132a8(mdo sde): thob pa 'gro ba nye bar 'tsho// de'i shes pa chags pa med pa yis// 'gro ba'i dogs pa dag ni gcod par byed// nan tan snying por byed pa'i rnal 'byor pa// dran dang bre gros rtogs dang
132b1(mdo sde): chos shes snang // bde ba'i snang ba mtha' yas// mngon par shes pa'i snang bar gyur pa yin// sgrib pas ye shes dang ni shes rab dang // rgyal chen blo dang spobs pa mtha' yas dang //
132b2(mdo sde): yang dag lta ba dang ni lhag mthong dang // shin tu 'khrugs pa med pa mthar thug gyur// snang ba shin tu rnam par dag pa brgyad// 'di dag mthu chen gang la yod pa ni// ri shig byang
132b3(mdo sde): chub thob par ma gyur kyang // de ni sangs rgyas mdzad pa byed par 'gyur// bcom ldan 'das kyis gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' gzungs kyi dbang phyug gi rgyal po la bka' stsal
132b4(mdo sde): pa/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnam pa bcu drug gis/ sems can rnams la byang chub sems dpa'i snying rje chen po skye'o// bcu drug gang zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di la byang chub
132b5(mdo sde): sems dpa' 'di snyam du/ kye ma sems can 'di dag ni 'jigs tshogs la lta bas bcings pa lta ba sna tshogs dang 'dres pa dag go// lta ba thams cad spang ba'i phyir de dag la chos ston
132b6(mdo sde): bar bya'o snyam du sems can rnams la byang chub sems dpa'i snying rje chen po skye ba dang // kye ma sems can 'di dag ni yod pa ma yin pa'i phyin ci log tu gyur nas/ mi rtag pa la rtag pa

166b2(mdo sde): rgyas kyi ting nge 'dzin ni byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin gyis zil gyis non to// byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin ni de bzhin gshegs pa 'di ting nge 'dzin gyis zil gyis non to// /
166b3(mdo sde): bzhin gshegs pa'i ting nge zil gyis mi non pa ste/ 'di la de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes ni zil byas mi non par 'jug go/ gdams pa gang dang rjes su bstan pa gang gis nyan
166b4(mdo sde): thos rnams ting nge 'dzin skyed pa de'ang de bzhin gshegs pas rab tu shes so de bzhin du rang sangs rgyas dang / de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi de dag kyang de bzhin gshegs
166b5(mdo sde): ba sa rab tu shes so// ga shes nas kyang de bzhin du 'dems shing de bzhin rjes su ston te/ 'di ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i las bdun pa'o// de la 'di skad ces bya'o// 'dir ni
166b6(mdo sde): 'gro ba kun nas nyon mongs rgyu dang rkyen// rgyal ba rang byang ye shes ldan pas de kun shes// de bzhin mngon par brtson rgyus rnam dag 'gyur ba'i// rgyu dang rkyen de chos kyi rjes ni rab
166b7(mdo sde): tu shes// nul bzhin ma yin rgyu ste rkyen ni ma rig pa// rgyu ni ma rig pa ste rkyen ni 'du byed yin// rnam par shes dang gzugs dang dbang po drug/ thams cad srid pa'i yan lag
166b8(mdo sde): 'gro ba'i rgyu dang rkyen/ nyon mongs rnams ni rgyu ste de bzhin las rnams rkyen// lta ba rgya ste de bzhin sred pa rkyen du gsungs// kun tu sbyor ba dang bag la nyal 'di 'dir rgyu ste// ming
167a1(mdo sde): / dang rgyu lasu kun tu 'byeng ba de 'di rkyen// 'gro ba rnam dag 'gyur ba'i rgyu dang rkyen ni gnyis po// gzhan las mthun pa'i sgra thos pa dang / thos nas kyang chos rnams

167a4(mdo sde): gyi sgo la sgom// zad pa dang ni mi skye shes dang bden pa thob// 'di ni rnam dag lam du 'dres pa'i rgyu dang rkyen// rgyal ba bsam gtan gcig la yang dag snyoms zhugs nas 'gog

167b7(mdo sde): gi sngon gyi gnas pa du ma rjes su dran no// de sems de'i sngon gyi gnas rjes su dran no// sngon gyi rgyu ji lta bu dang rgyu ga rigs sems can gang gis tu byung ba de'i sngon gyi rgyu de bzhin gshegs
167b8(mdo sde): pas rab tu shes te/ shes nas kyang de bzhin du chos ston/ 'das pa'i sems can thams cad kyi sems kyi rgyu ba yang de bzhin gshegs pas rab tu shes so// sems kyi rimag

9a1(mdo sde): dri za'i bu mo brgya phrag du ma dag 'tshogs so// 'khor der mi 'am ci'i bu mo brgya phrag du ma dag 'tshogs pa 'di lta ste/
9a2(mdo sde): mi 'am ci'i bu mo yid byed ces bya ba dang / mi 'am ci'i bu mo yid las byung zhes bya ba dang / mi 'am ci'i bu mo rlung gis shugs zhes bya ba dang / mi 'am ci'i
9a3(mdo sde): bu mo chu'i shugs shes bya ba dang / mi 'am ci'i bu mo na mkha'i gzings shes bya ba dang / mi 'am ci'i bu mo mgyogs pa'i shugs shes bya ba dang / mi'i
9a4(mdo sde): ci'i bu mo dpal sbyin zhes bya ba dang / mi 'am ci bu mo mche ba bzang mo zhes bya ba dang / mi 'am ci'i bu mo mi g.yo ba'i dpal zhes bya ba dang / mi 'am ci'i bu mo
9a5(mdo sde): khams la dga' zhes bya ba dang / mi 'am ci'i bu mo 'bar ba la dga' ba zhes bya ba dang / mi 'am ci'i bu mo shin tu dpal zhes bya ba dang / mi 'am ci'i bu mo
9a6(mdo sde): rin po chos 'byung gnas shes bya ba dang / mi 'am ci'i bu mo spyan ras gzigs kyi dpal zhes bya ba dang / mi 'am ci'i bu mo stan can zhes bya ba dang / mi 'am ci
9a7(mdo sde): bu me rdo rje'i khu tshur zhes bya ba dang / mi 'am ci'i bu mo ser ske zhes bya ba dang / mi 'am ci'i bu mo rgyan rab rgyan pa zhes bya ba dang / mi 'am ci 'bu mo 'phral
9a8(mdo sde): ba dpes chen zhes bya ba dang / mi 'am ci'i bu mo nges pa yongs su bsten pa zhes bya ba dang / mi 'am ci'i bu mo blo gros chen mo zhes bya ba dang / mi 'am ci'i bu
9b1(mdo sde): mo na mkha' srung zhes bya ba dang / mi 'am ci'i bu mo bkod pa rgyal po'i dbang zhes bya ba dang / mi 'am ci'i bu mo gtsug na nor bu zhes bya ba dang / mi 'am
9b2(mdo sde): ci'i bu me nor bu 'dzin ces bya ba dang / mi 'am ci'i bu mo nor bu 'bar ba zhes bya ba dang / mi 'am ci'i bu mo skye bo 'khas pa sten pas bya ba dang / mi'i
9b3(mdo sde): ci'i bu mo mdogs ma zhes bya ba dang / mi 'am ci'i bu mo tshe sbyin zhes bya ba dang / mi 'am ci'i bu mo de bzhin gshegs pa'i mdzod yongs su skong ma zhes bya ba dang /
9b4(mdo sde): mi 'am ci'i bu me chos kyi dbyings yongs su srung ba zhes bya ba dang / mi 'am ci'i bu mo rkang pi gdub bu zhes bya ba dang / mi 'am ci'i bu mo skad cig sbre l-i zhes
9b5(mdo sde): bya ba dang / mi 'am ci'i mo rtag tu chos len par 'dod ces bya ba dang / mi 'am ci'i bu mo rtag tu dus dus su ston ma zhes bya ba dang / mi 'am ci'i bu mo
9b6(mdo sde): dbugs 'byin ces bya ba dang / mi 'am ci'i bu mo rnam par thar byed ces bya ba dang / mi 'am ci'i bu mo yid mi 'phrogs pa zhes bya ba dang / mi 'am tswi
9b7(mdo sde): bu mo skye 'dzin ces bya ba dang / mi 'ami ci'i bu mo rol gyi 'bar ba zhes bya ba dang / mi 'am ci'i bu mo sa las 'gro zhes bya ba dang / mi 'am ci'i bu mo lha dbang 'phreng
9b8(mdo sde): ba zhes bya ba dang / mi 'am ci'i bu mo lha ma yin gyi dbang mo zhes bya ba dang / mi'i ci'i bu mo nor bu dbang zhes zhes bya ba dang / mi 'am ci'i bu mo rus bzod ces
10a1(mdo sde): bya ba dang / mi 'am ci'i bu mo sbyin ldan zhes bya ba dang / mi 'am ci'i bu mo dbang pos gnas shes bya ba dang / mi 'am ci bu mo lag ca brgya pa
10a2(mdo sde): zhes bya ba dang / mi 'am ci'i bu mo rgyan gyis rgyan ces bya ba dang / mi 'am ci'i bu mo yid 'phrogs zhes bya ba dang / de lta bu las stsogs pa mi 'am ci'i bu mo
10a3(mdo sde): brgya phrag du ma dag 'tshog so// dge bsnyen ma brgya phrag du ma dag 'chog so// mur 'dag spyod pa dang / kun tu rgyu ba dang / gcer bu pa brgya phrag du ma dag kyang 'tshog ste/
10a4(mdo sde): gAr+b+hen 'dus pa ni gyur pa de'i tshe na/ sems can dmyal ba chen po man med par 'od zer bya // byung nas mdze ti'i tshal gyi gtsug khung du song ba dang / de dgas
10a5(mdo sde): gtsug lag khang de yongs su mdzes par snang ste/ ka ba ni lha'i nor bu rin pe cos brgyan par snang // rtsigs pa brgya dag kyang gser gyis mdzes par byas pa snango //
10a6(mdo sde): gnas khang so so dag na ni drang dngul las byas sgo dag snang ngo // gnas khang so so na skas gser dang dngul las byas pa dag kyang snang ngo do// dngul gyi khang pa dag ni ni gse
10a7(mdo sde): byi ka ba rin po ci rgyan pa dang / gswe gyi khang pa dag na ni dngul gyi ka ba rin po che brgyan pa dang / mdze ti'i tshal gyi phyi ro la na shing sngags bsam ni pa sna tshogs dag snang ste/ gse
10a8(mdo sde): gyi sdong po dang / rdul gyi lo ma dang / rgyan pa sna tshogs rab tu 'phyang ba dag dang / yul ka shi ka nas byung ba'i gos rab tu 'phyang ba dag dang / rmyi gos brgya rab tu 'phyang ba dag dang
10b1(mdo sde): mu tig gi se mo dog brgya stong rab tu 'phyang ba dag kyang / cod pan dang rna ca dang 'phreng ba'i lda ldi dang / dpung rgyan dang / rkang pa'i gdu bu rab tu 'phyang ba dang / phyi rol ni rin po/
10b2(mdo sde): che'i gdu bu stong rin po che las byas pi de dag 'phyang ba'i shing dpag bsam gyi shing de lta bu dag kyang byung ngo // mdze ti tshal gyi gtsug lag khang de nyid na/ sa skas dag kyang
10b3(mdo sde): rdo rje las byas par snang / sgo rgya bo na mri tig dang / dar gyi tshogs rab tu spangaso// rdzing bu du ma dag kyang byang ste/ la la chu'i yan lag brgyad dang ldan pas yongs su gang /
10b4(mdo sde): la la ni me tog rnam pa sna tshogs kyis yongs gang ba dag 'di lta ste/ me tog ud pa la dang / pad ma dang / ku mu da dang / pun da ri ka dang / man da ra ba dang / man da ra ba chen po
10b5(mdo sde): dang / a dum par dag gis yongasu gang ngo // gzhan yang shing gi me tog rnam pa sna tshogs skye ba 'di lta ste/ me ga me tog tsam pa ka dang / ka ra bi ra dang / pa ta la la dang /
10b6(mdo sde): ad ti mu ta ka dang / dbyar gyi dr-i dang / gzhan yang shing gi me tog yid dga' ba dag 'byung ste/ mdze ta'i tshal gyi gtsug lag khang de yongs su mdzes par byas pa nyid du
10b7(mdo sde): snang ngo // de nas 'khor de nyid kyi nang du/ byang chub sems dpa sgrib pa thams cad rnam par sel ba stan las langs te/ bla gos phrag pa gcig tu gzar nas pus mo g.yas
10b8(mdo sde): pAlI nga sa la btsug te/ bcom ldan 'das ga la ba de ldog su thal mo sbar ba bted/ bco ldan 'dra la 'di skad ces gsol to// bco ldan 'das bdag ni shin tu ngo maT+Tarma du byung ba the bo//
11a1(mdo sde): bcom ldan 'das 'od zer chen po 'di dag ga las mchis/ rdzu 'phrul gyi yul gyi mthu 'di su'i lags/ bcom ldan 'das kyis
11a2(mdo sde): bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang po 'di ni mnar med pa'i sems can dmyal ba chen por zhugs nas/ sems can rnam
11a3(mdo sde): la yongs su smin par byed de/ yongasu smin par byas nas/ yi dgas kyi grong khyer du 'jug go// de nas bcom ldan 'das la/ byang chub sems dpa' sgrib pa
11a4(mdo sde): thams cad rnam par sel bas 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das mnar ma mchis pa'i sems can dmyal ba chen po na mnar ba rim gda' na/ bcom ldan
11a5(mdo sde): 'das ji ltar na/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang po 'jug par bgyid/ sems can dmyal ba chen po lcags kyi rtsigs/
11a6(mdo sde): pas bskor la/ lcags kyi dog sa la shin tu 'bar ba me lce gcig tu 'dus pa rnam par g.yo ba de na/ 'bod sgrogs pa dag gnas pa'i snod za ma tog 'dra ba
11a7(mdo sde): mchis te/ snod der sems can bye ba khrag khrig rgya stong phrag du ma skul to// nam chu mang po mchis pa'i snod na/ sran chung ka ru 'am/ na gu gyen tu mchi na yang /
11a8(mdo sde): gral ba dang smin par 'gyur/ thur du mitsha na 'ang gral ba dang / smin par 'gyur ba de bzhin du/ sems can de dag kyang mnar ma mchis pa'i sems can dmyal
11b1(mdo sde): pa chen po dar/ lus kyi sdug bsngal nyams su myong na/ bcom ldan 'das ji ltar na/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang po//
11b2(mdo sde): mnar med pa'i sems can dmyal ba chen por 'jug par bgyid/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu ji ltar na/ 'khor lo sgyur ba'i rgyal po lha'i
11b3(mdo sde): bu nor bu rin po che las byas pa'i skyes mos tshal du 'jug pa de bzhin du/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang po yang / mnar med pa'i
11b4(mdo sde): sems can dmyal ba chen por 'jug mod kyi/ de'i lus la gzhan du 'byur ba med do// nam mnar med pa'i sems can dmyal ba chen po dang / nye bar 'gro ba de'i tshe/
11b5(mdo sde): mnar med pa'i sems can dmyal ba chen po de bsil bar gyur te/ de'i tshe ga shin rje'i mi de dag mnar med pa'i sems can dmyal ba chen po ci mi dge ba'i ltas shig byung na
11b6(mdo sde): nam byang chub sems dpa' spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang po 'ongs pa de'i tshe/ me tog pad ma shing rta'i 'khor lo tsam byang zhing snod de yang bsal/ me'i 'obs
11b7(mdo sde): de nyid du yang rdzing bu byung bar gyur ces skyo bar gyur to// de nas gshin rje'i skyes bu de dag ral gri dang / gtun dang mchin cha 'byin ti pa la dang / to ma ra dang /
11b8(mdo sde): 'khor lo dang / rtse gsum las stsogs pa thogs nas/ ga shin rje'i rgyal po ga la ba der song ste phyin nas/ 'di skad ces smras so// lha bdag gis su
12a1(mdo sde): las kyi ngogs de yongs su bas par mkhyen par mdzod cig/ de'i phyir khyed kyi ltas kyi yongs su zad/ lha ci lags mi mkhyen
12a2(mdo sde): nam/ mnar ma mchis pI sems can dmyal ba der thogs ma kho nar mi dge ba'i ltas byung ste/ skyes bu ji ltar 'dod pa'i gzugs can/ ral pa'i cod
12a3(mdo sde): pan can/ lus rgyan thams cad kyis rgyan pa phyin pa dang bsil bar 'gyur ro// gang gi tshe der phyin pa de'i tshe/ me tog pad ma shing rta'i 'khor lo tsam yang
12a4(mdo sde): byung snod de yang gas/ zhugs kyi 'obs der yang rdzing bu byung bar gyur to// de nas gshin rje'i rgyal po sems par gyur te/ mthu 'di lta gang gi yin/ yang na
12a5(mdo sde): lha'i bu dbang phyug chen po dang / mthu bo che las dam pa thob pa zhig sa 'dir 'ongs sam/ ya na srin po mthu bo che lha'i ban lang gi stobs dang 'dren pa nyid skyes
12a6(mdo sde): sam zhes des lha'i mig gis rnam par bltas na/ lha'i sde'i nang na dam pa de lta bu ma mthong ngo // de nas slar yang mnar med pa'i sems can dmyal ba chen por
12a7(mdo sde): bltas so// der bltas pa dang mnar med pa'i sems can dmyal ba chen po de na/ byang chub sems dpa' sman ras gzigs kyi dbang po bzhugs pa nyid du
12a8(mdo sde): mthong ngo // de nas gshin rje'i rgyal po byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ga la ba der song ste phyin pa dang / bcom ldan 'das kyis zhabs la mag/
12b1(mdo sde): mgo bos phyag 'tshal nas/ bstod pa'i khyed par byed par rtsom pa/ spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang phyug chen po/ pad ma la dgyes pa pad ma stsol ba dbang du mdzad pa/
12b2(mdo sde): sa'i sman dam pa mdzad/ dbugs 'byin par mdzad pa/ phyag chu sdong pa sman bye ba brgya srong dbu bcu gcig pa/ dgod ma'i bzhin lta bu'i mthar phyin pa chos la dgyes pa//
12b3(mdo sde): sems can thams cad yongs su thar par mdzad pa/ ru sbal dang chu srin dang / nya rnams dbugs 'byin par mdzad pa/ ye shes kyi phung po dam pa mdzad pa/ dga' ba stsol ba/
12b4(mdo sde): rin po che'i dpal dam pa/ mnar med pa'i kun skems par mdzad pa/ ye shes kyis dpal gyis brgyan pa/ ye shes la dgyes pa/ lha thams cad kyis mchod pa/
12b5(mdo sde): phyag 'tshal ba/ ba ku ra sti bgyis pa/ mi 'jigs gsol pa/ pha rol tu phyin pa drug ston par mdzad pa/ nyi ma lta bu'i sman mchog mdzad pa chos kyi sgron ma mdzad pa/
12b6(mdo sde): ji ltar dgyes pa'i gzugs kyi gzugs mchog/ dri za'i gzugs dang ldan pa/ gser gyi ri'i gzugs dang mtshungs pa/ rgya mtsho 'ching rnams kyi rnams khong bzhin
12b7(mdo sde): du zab pa/ don dam pa'i rnal 'byor rjes su thob pa/ bdag gi zhal ston par mdzad pa/ ting nge 'dzin brgya stong du ma dang ldan pa/ mngon par dgyes par mdzad pa/
12b8(mdo sde): sku brgyan pa/ skyes bu khyu mchog khung sgo dang / khong sgril dang / 'khrul 'khor gyis lam las yongs su thar bar mdzad pa/ srid pa thams cad dang ma 'brel ba/
13a1(mdo sde): 'khor mang po 'byung bar gyur pa bsags pa/ yid bzhin gyi nor bu rin po che mdzad pa/ mya ngan las 'das pa'i lam ston par mdzad pa/
13a2(mdo sde): yi dgas kyi grong khyer skyems par mdzad pa/ skye bo la gdug su gyur par mdzad pa/ nad las yongasu mthar par mdzad pa/ klu'i rgyal po dga' bo dang bsnyen dga' bo
13a3(mdo sde): mchog sprin thogs pa/ don yod par 'gyur ba'i zhags pa ston par mdzad pa/ sngags brgya phrag du ma dang ldan pa/ lag na rdo rje skrag par mdzad pa/ 'jig rten gsuM
13a4(mdo sde): skrag par mdzad pa/ gnod sbyin dang / srin po dang / 'byung po dang / sha za dang / 'phra men ma dang / 'phra men pa dang / ro ya langs dang / grul bum dang /
13a5(mdo sde): rjod byeng rnams skrag par mdzad pa/ spun ud pa la sngon po lta bu zab cing brtan par mdzad pa/ rigs pa'i bdag po nyon mongs pa thams cad las rnam par grol bar
13a6(mdo sde): mdzad pa/ lem sna tshogs bsags pa/ thar pa'i dam pa la zhugs pa/ sku la byang chub kyi lam bsags pa/ yi dgas yongs su thar par mdzad pa/ ting
13a7(mdo sde): de 'dzin rdul phra rab lta bu brgya stong dang ldan pa la phyag 'tshal lo zhes de ltar gshin rje'i rgyal pos khyed par dam pa ston pas stod nas/ slar yang gshin rje'i rgyal pos lan
13a8(mdo sde): gsum bskor de de nyid nas song ngo // de nas bcom ldan 'das la byang chub sems dpa' sgrib pa thams cad rnam par sel bas 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan
13b1(mdo sde): 'das byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang po 'chi 'am/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu de ni mnar med
13b2(mdo sde): pa'i sems can dmyal bar chen po nas byung ste/ yi dgas kyi grong khyer du song nas 'gal shing lta bu dang / keng rus sgreng pa dang / bdag gis skra dang sngas yog pa
13b3(mdo sde): dang / lte ri dang 'dra ba dang / kha khab kyi mig lta bu'i yi dgas rgya stong du mdun na rgyug go// byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po spun ras gzigs kyi
13b4(mdo sde): dbang po nam yi dgas kyi grong khyer du song ba de'i tshe/ yi dgas kyi grong khyer de bsil bar 'gyur/ rdo rje'i ser ba de yang rab tu zhi bar 'gyur ro// sgo ba de yang yin pa
13b5(mdo sde): thag thugs can dmigs dmar zhing lag na 'khar ba thogs pa/ las kyi sa 'di 'dra ba ni bdag gi bya ba ma yin no zhes byams pa'i sems skyed do// de nas byang chub sems
13b6(mdo sde): dpa' sems dpa' chen po spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang po'i phyag gi sor mo bcu las chu bo chen po bcu byung / zhabs kyi sor mo bcu las chu bo chen po bcu byung ste/ byang
13b7(mdo sde): chub sems dpa' spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang po shin tu thugs rtse ba'i zil gyis gnon nas/ ba spre'i khung bu nas chu byung ngo // gang gi tshe na de dag gi chu meng ba de'i rga
13b8(mdo sde): de dag mgrin gcig pa yangs par gyur/ lus kyang yongasu rdzogs par/ lha'i zas ro'i nang na mchog tu byang ba dang ldan pas tshim par yang gyur nas/ de'i tshe 'khor
14a1(mdo sde): ba'i bsam pa la sems te/ kye ma'o 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi 'di dag ni/ grib ma bsil ba la yongasu ston to// gang mdzam bu'i gling gi
14a2(mdo sde): mi 'di dag ni/ rtag tu pha dang ma la yongs su 'dzin cing snyen bkur byed de bde ba dang ldan pa'o// gang rtag tu dge ba'i bshes gnyen dang sten cing skyong ba'i skyes bu de
14a3(mdo sde): dag ni bde ba dang ldan pa'o// gang rtag tu theg pa chen po rtag tu khong du chud par byed par byed pa'i skyes bu dam pa de dag ni bsam pa ldan pa'o// gang 'phags pa'i
14a4(mdo sde): lam yan lag brgyad pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa gnas par byed pa de dag ni skyes bu dam pa'o// gang chos kyi 'gan de rdung ba de dag ni skyes bu dam pa'o// gang gtsug
14a5(mdo sde): lag khang gso ba dang / gogs pa rnams slar 'chos pa de ni skyes bu dam pa'o// gang sngon mchod rten gyi gzugs gas pa dang gogs pa rnams slar mchos pa de dag ni skyes
14a6(mdo sde): bu dam pa'o// gang smra ba dang sten pa de dag ni skyes bu dam pa'o// gang de bzhin gshegs pa 'chag pa mthong ba de dag ni skyes bu dam pa'o// gang rang sangs rgyas
14a7(mdo sde): 'chag pa mthong ba de dag ni skyes bu dam pa'o// gang byang chub sems dpa' 'chag pa mthong ba de ni skyes bu dam pa'o// zhes de ltar lus kyis rjes su sems pa dang
14a8(mdo sde): de'i tshe theg pa chen po mdo za mo tog bkod pa bkon mchog gsum po'i sgra byung ngo // de'i tshe dag gi 'jig tshogs su lta ba'i rtse mo nyi shu byung ba// ye shes kyi rdo rjes
14b1(mdo sde): bcom nas/ de dag thams cad bde ba can du 'jig rten gyi khams su skyes te/ byang chub sems dpa' 'dod pa'i bzhin zhes bya bar skye nas/ gang gi tshe des
14b2(mdo sde): sems can yongs su smin par byas pa de'i tshe slar yang song ngo // de nas bcom ldan 'das la sgrib pa thams cad rnam pari sel bas 'di skad ces gsol to// /
14b3(mdo sde): bco ga 'ad byang dub ses dag mi sa dpa med pa skyed sa bi ba dbang bya'adi 'ag ba sa 'das byes pa bstsal pa'i kyi bunyis zhing se bapas byeg thag leg pa ltang dus 'ongs med bye 'i 'i grong ra bya gyu sem sa mes dadu brgya na 'i ba'i sgom me shin byesas 'ad
14b4(mdo sde): sgrib pa thams cad rnam par sel bas gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das ci'i slad du bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu de bzhin gshegs pa
14b5(mdo sde): dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas lhag mthong zhes bya ba rig pa dang rkang pa ldan pa bde bar gshegs pa/ 'jig rten mkhyen pa skyes bu 'dul ba'i
14b6(mdo sde): kha lo sgyur ba/ lha dang mi rnams kyi ston pa sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das sngon 'jig rten du 'byung bar gyur to// de'i tshe de'i dus na sgrib pa thams cad rnam por sel
14b7(mdo sde): pa de ni spos kyi gzhi zhes bya ba'i tshong ba'i bur 'gyur te/ de'i tshe ngas de bzhin gshegs pa'i lhag mthong las spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang po'i yon tan brjod pa
14b8(mdo sde): thos so// de nas bcom ldan 'das la sgrib pa thams cad rnam par sel bas 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa' sems
15a1(mdo sde): dpa' chen po spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang po'i yon tan brjod pa ji skad du gsan/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ mig la
15a2(mdo sde): nyi ma dang zla ba byung ba/ bral ba la sa dbang phyug chen po/ phrag pa las ni tshangs pa/ snying las ni thu bo che/ mche ba gnyis las ni lha mo// kha nas ni rlung rnams
15a3(mdo sde): 'byung / rkang pa las sa/ lto las ni chu'i lha 'byung ste/ gang gi tshe spun ras gzigs kyi dbang po'i lus las lha de dag byung ba de'i tshe/ bcom ldan 'das
15a4(mdo sde): kyis lha'i bu dbang phyug chen po la 'di skad ces gsungs te/ dbang phyug chen po khyod/ dus ngan pa'i sems can gyi khams ma rung ba dag byung ba na khyod thog mar byed pa po gton
15a5(mdo sde): ba po'i lhar grags par 'gyur ro// sems can de dag ni/ byang chub kyi lam yongasu sbyangs par 'gyur ro// so so'i skye bo'i nang de ni/ na mkha'i de'i rtags so// sa
15a6(mdo sde): ni de'i khri'o// sems can thams cad kyi gnas so// zhi bar 'gyur ba ni rtag so// zhes zer bar 'gyur ro zhes rigs kyi bu ngas de bzhin bya lhag mthong las
15a7(mdo sde): de skad thos so// de yang 'das nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas gtsug ldan zhes bya ba rig pa dang rkang par ldan pa
15a8(mdo sde): bde bar gshegs pa/ 'jig rten mkhyen pa/ skyes bu 'dul ba'i kha lo sgyur ba/ lha dang mi rnams kyi ston pa/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de'i tshe de'i dus/
15b1(mdo sde): na/ sgrib pa thams cad rnam par sel ba nga ni byang chub sbyin pa zhes bya bar 'gyur te/ de las kyang ngas byang chub sems dpa' spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang po'i yon tan
15b2(mdo sde): rjod pa thos so// de nas bcom ldan 'das la sgrib pa thams cad rnam par sel bas/ 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa'
15b3(mdo sde): sems dpa' chen po spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang po'i yon tan rjod pa ji skad du gsan/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ lha dang klu dang / gnod sbyin dang /
15b4(mdo sde): lha ma yin dang / lto 'phye chen po dang / mi thams cad 'dus par gyur te/ gang gi tshe na bcom ldan 'das kyis 'dus pa chen po gzigs nas/ 'khor de'i nang na
15b5(mdo sde): chos kyis gtam bya bar rtsams pa de'i tshe/ bcom ldan 'das kyis zhal gyi sgo nas/ 'od zer gyi kha dog sna tshogs byung ba/ sngon po dang / ser po dang / dmar po
15b6(mdo sde): dang / dkar po dang / rnga 'od dang / shel dang / de rdul gyi kha dog rnams byung ste/ phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du snang bar byas nas/ slar
15b7(mdo sde): 'ongs te bskor nus/ bcom ldan 'das kyis zhal gyi sgor song / de nas 'khor der/ byang chub sems dpa' lag na rin po che stan las langs te/
15b8(mdo sde): gos phrag pa gcig la gzar nas/ pus mo g.yas pa'i lha nga sa la btsug te/ bcom ldan 'das ga la ba der logs su thal mo sbar ba btad nas/ btso
16a1(mdo sde): ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das ci'i slad du ltas 'di lta bu stan par 'gyur/ bcom ldan 'das kyis
16a2(mdo sde): bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po spyan ras gzigs kyi blo de 'jig rten gyi khams bde ba can du 'ongs te/ de 'ong ba'i tshe ltas
16a3(mdo sde): 'di 'dra ba bstan to// gang gi tshe byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po spyan ras kyi dbang po 'ong ba de'i tshe/ shing dpag sems rnams kyang 'phel bar 'gyur//
16a4(mdo sde): shing tsu ta ka yang 'phel bar 'gyur/ shing kun da'i me tog kyang 'byung bar 'gyur/ shing tsam pa ka yang 'phyang bar 'gyur/ rdzing bu me teg gis shin tu gang ba yang
16a5(mdo sde): 'byung bar 'gyur te/ de las rin po che'i shing rnams kyang 'byung bar 'gyur ro// char sna tshogs kyang 'bab par 'gyur te/ nor bu dang / mu tig dang / bye du r+ya dang /
16a6(mdo sde): dung dang / man shel dang / byi ru dang / rin po che'i char yang 'bab/ lha'i gos kyi char yang 'bab par 'gyur ro// lha gang de dang nye ba nyid du rin po che'i bdun yod
16a7(mdo sde): byung ba/ 'di lta ste 'khor lo rin po che dang / bal glang rin po che dang / rta rin po che dang / nor bu che rin po dang / bud med rin po che dang / khyim bdagi ran
16a8(mdo sde): po che dang / blon po rin po che bdun rnams so// de dag byung nas sa gser du snang ngo // gang gi tshe byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po spun ras gzig
16b1(mdo sde): kyi dbang po 'jig rten gyi khams bde ba can nas byung ba de'i tshe/ sa rnam pa drug tu g.yos so// de nas bcom ldan 'das la byang chub sems dpa' lag na rdo rjes 'di/
16b2(mdo sde): skad ces gsol te// bcom ldan 'das gang gi ltas lags/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' spyan ras gzigs
16b3(mdo sde): kyi dbang po de 'ongs te/ de'i ltas 'di 'dra ba dag byung ngo // gang gi tshe na skyed pa de'i tshe/ yid dga' ba'i me tog pad ma'i char rab tu phab ste/ de'i tshe byang chub
16b4(mdo sde): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang pos/ me tog pad ma 'dab ma stong pa sdong pu gser du snang ba thogs nas/ bcom ldan 'das pa
16b5(mdo sde): la ba der song ste phyin pa dang / bcom ldan 'das kyis zhabs la 'go bos phyag 'tshal te/ me tog 'di dag de bzhin gshegs pa sna ba mtha' yas kyis
16b6(mdo sde): bskar ro zhes pad ma phul te/ bsnyung ba ma mchis sam/ 'o ma brgyal tam/ bzhengs pa yang ngam/ reg par gsan sam zhes kyang gsung ngo // de nas pad ma blangs te/
16b7(mdo sde): g.yon phyog su bzhags nas/ de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang po'i yon tan brjod pa mdzad do// spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang po las kyi sa
16b8(mdo sde): ji lta bur bsgrubs pa yin/ sems can yi dgas dang / stir med par skyes pa dag/ thig nag po can dag dang / 'o dod 'bod pa dag dang / ha ha zhes 'bod pa zas
17a1(mdo sde): cad dang / gdung ba'i sems can dmyal ba chen po dang / me'i bum pa'i sems can dmyal ba chen po sham pa la dang / sems can
17a2(mdo sde): dmyal ba chen po chu grang ba dang / sems can dmyal ba chen po de dag tu sems can gang dag skyes pa de dag ni bdag las kyis ste/ bdag gi sems can yongs su
17a3(mdo sde): smin par bgyi'o// bgyis nas bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub la bgod par bgyi'o// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po spyan
17a4(mdo sde): ras gzigs kyi dbang pos dri ba'i lan btab nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyis zhabs la mgo bos phyag 'tshal te/ phyogs gcig tu song // song nas ma
17a5(mdo sde): phung po 'bar ba bzhin du na mkha' la ni mi snang bar song ngo // de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po lag na rin pon ces 'di skad ces gsol to// /
17a6(mdo sde): bcom ldan 'das zhu ba lung stan pa bshad pa bdag zhu na/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang po'i bsod nams kyi tshogs
17a7(mdo sde): lta bu lags/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas gang gi'i klung gi bye ma snyed la lha'i skal
17a8(mdo sde): par na bza' dang / bshos dang / na pa'i rkyen sman dang / yo byed rnams kyis bsnyen bkur byas nas/ gang de bzhin gshegs de dag las bsod nams 'phel bar
17a9(mdo sde): papal bstan dang /
17b1(mdo sde): 'gyur ba'i bsod nams de/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang po'i baspu gcig gi rtse mo la gnas so// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/
17b2(mdo sde): gling chen po bzhir zla ba bcu gnyis kyi lor nyin mtshan du char bab kyang thigs pa re re nas bgrang nus kyi/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po spyan ras gzig
17b3(mdo sde): kyi dbang po'i bsod nams kyi tshogs ni ngas bgrang bar mi nus so// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ rgya mtsho'i 'ching rnams chen po zabs su dpag tshad brgyad khro bzhi stong yod
17b4(mdo sde): la/ zheng du dpag tu med la/ rta dgod ma'i kha lta bu'i mthar thugs pa'i thigs pa re re nas ngas bgrangs nus kyi/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa chen
17b5(mdo sde): po spun ras gzigs kyi dbang po'i bsod nams kyi tshogs ni ngas bgrangs par mi nus so// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ gling chen po bzhin/ seng ges dang stag dang /
17b6(mdo sde): dred dang / ta rag sha ga dang / ri dgas las stsogs pa ba glang dang / bong bu dang / phyag dang / bal glang dang / rta dang ma he dang / byi la las stsogs pa rkang bzhi
17b7(mdo sde): pa de dag gi spu re re nas ngas bgrang nus kyi rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang po'i bsod nams kyi tshogs kyi grangs bgrang bar
17b8(mdo sde): mi nus so// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ rdul phra rab kyi rdul snyed kyi de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams lha'i gser rin po che
18a1(mdo sde): las byas nas nyin gcig tu ring srel bcug na/ rigs kyi bu de'i bsod nams kyi phung po ni nges pa grang nus kyi/ byang chub sems dpa'
18a2(mdo sde): sems dpa' chen po spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang po'i bsod nams kyi tshogs bgrang bar mi nus so// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ shing shri sha ba'i tshal gyi lo ma ni ngas
18a3(mdo sde): bgrang nus kyi/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang po'i bsod nams kyi tshogs na bgrang mi nus so// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/
18a4(mdo sde): gling chen po bzhin gnas pa'i skyes pa dang bud med dang / khye'u dang bu mo gnas pa de dag thams cad rgyun tu zhugs pa'i 'bras bu dang / lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu dang /
18a5(mdo sde): phyir mi ldog pa'i 'bras bu dang / dgra bcom pa dang / rang byang chub la bkod na/ gang de dag gi bsod nams kyi phung po ni snga ma bzhin du/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa
18a6(mdo sde): chen po'i ba spa'i rtse mo'i bsod nams kyi phung po dang mnyam mo// de nas bcom ldan 'das la/ byang chub sems dpa' lag na rin po ches 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom
18a7(mdo sde): ldan 'das bdag ni byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang po'i bsod nams kyi phung po ci 'dra ba de lta bu/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnams la
18a8(mdo sde): yang gang na yang mthong ma thos na/ byang chub sems dpar gyur pa lta ci smos/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu gang nga dang 'dra ba'i de bzhin gshegs/
18b1(mdo sde): bang gra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams su gyur la/ de dag kyang gnas gcig tu gzhog cing na bza' dang / bshos dang / mal stan dang / na pa'i rkye
18b2(mdo sde): sman dang / yo byed rnams kyis skal par gzhog cing / de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas de dag gis/ byang chub sems dpa' sem
18b3(mdo sde): dpa' chen po spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang po'i bsod nams kyi phung po bgrang mi nus na/ rigs kyi bu da gcig pu 'jig rten gyi khams 'di na gnas pas lta ci smos/ gang
18b4(mdo sde): 'jig rten na spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang po'i ming dran pa de dag gi bde ba dang ldan pa yin no// de dag ni dga' dang 'chi ba dang na ba dang / sdug bsngal dang yongs su thar pa yino//
18b5(mdo sde): de dag na 'khor ba'i tha ma gzhan med pa'i sdug bsngal bar ma 'gyur ro// de dag ni gos dkar po dang skya bo bzhin du bya dang pa dang rgyal po mgyogs pa dang / rlung gi shugs 'ongs pa
18b6(mdo sde): bzhin du/ bde ba can gyi 'jig rten gyi khams su de bzhin gshegs pa snang ba mtha' yas las chos mngon du nyan pa'i phyir 'gro'o// thos nas kyang de dag gi lus la 'khor ba'i/
18b7(mdo sde): sdug bsngal mi 'byung / 'dod chags dang zhe sdang dang gti mug mi 'byung / dgas pa dang shi bar mi 'gyur/ de dag gi lus la bkres par mi 'gyur/ mngal na gnas pa'i
18b8(mdo sde): sdig bsngal ba shes ngar mi 'gyur te/ chos kyi ches bskyed nas de nyid du bang ma'i nang du skye bar 'gyur te/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po spun ras gzigs kyi sa
19a1(mdo sde): po'i yid dam brtan yongs su rdzogs pa dang / sems can thams cad thar pa la bzhag gi bar du 'jig rten gyi khams de na rtag tu 'dzin
19a2(mdo sde): cing gnas so// de nas bcom ldan 'das la byang chub sems dpa' lag na rin pos ches 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das gang gi dus na yid dam rten pa de
19a3(mdo sde): yongs su rdzogs pa lags/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ sems can mang po 'khor ba na 'khor ba'i sems can de dag yongasu smin par byed pa dang /
19a4(mdo sde): byang chub kyi lam ston par byed cing / gang dang gang gi gzugs kyis 'dul ba'i sems can rnams dul bar 'gyur ba de dang de'i gzugs kyis chos 'chad de/ de bzhin
19a5(mdo sde): gshegs pas 'dul ba'i sems can rnams la ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i gzugs kyis chos 'chad/ rang sangs rgyas kyis 'dul ba'i sems can rnams la ni/
19a6(mdo sde): rang sangs rgyas kyi gzugs kyi chos 'chad/ dgra bcom pas 'dul ba'i sems can rnams la ni/ dgra bcom pa'i gzugs kyi chos 'chad/ byang chub sems dpas
19a7(mdo sde): 'dul ba'i sems can rnams la ni// byang chub sems dpa'i gzugs kyis chos 'chad/ dbang phyug chen pos 'dul ba'i sems can rnams la ni/ dbang phyug chen
19a8(mdo sde): po'i gzugs kyi chos 'chad/ mthu bo ches 'dul ba'i sems can rnams la ni/ mthu bo che'i gzugs kyi chos 'chad/ tshangs pas 'dul ba'i sems can rnams la
19b1(mdo sde): ni/ tshangs pa'i gzugs kyis 'chad/ dbang pos 'dul ba'i sems can rnams ni/ dbang po'i gzugs kyis chos 'chad/ nyi mas 'dul ba'i sems can rnams
19b2(mdo sde): la ni/ nyi ma'i gzugs kyis chos 'chad/ zla bas 'dul ba'i sems can rnams la ni/ zla ba'i gzugs kyis chos 'chad/ me lhas 'dul ba'i sems can rnam
19b3(mdo sde): la ni/ me lha'i gzugs kyis chos 'chade/ chu lha'i gzugs kyis 'dul ba'i sems can rnams la ni/ chu lha'i gzugs kyis 'chad/ rlung lha'i 'dul ba'i sems
19b4(mdo sde): can rnams la ni rlung lha'i gzugs kyis chos 'chad/ klus 'dul ba'i sems can rnams la ni/ klu'i gzugs kyis chos 'chad/ bgegs med pa'i bdag pos

19b6(mdo sde): gzugs kyis chos 'chad/ ngal ba so bo'i gzugs kyis 'dul ba'i sems can rnams la ni/ ngal ba so bo'i gzugs kyis chos 'chad/ rgyal po'i gzugs kyis/
19b7(mdo sde): 'dul ba'i sems can rnams la ni/ rgyal po'i gzugs kyis chos 'chad/ pha dang mas 'dul ba'i sems can rnams la ni/ pha dang ma'i gzugs kyis chos 'chad
19b8(mdo sde): sems can dag ji lta ji ltar 'dul ba/ de lta de ltar chos ston to// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po spyan ras gzigs kyis dbang po ni/
20a1(mdo sde): de ltar sems can yongs su smin par byed cing / mya ngan las 'da' ba'i chos ston to// de nas bcom ldan 'das la byang chub sems dpa'

20a3(mdo sde): par ma gyur te/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang po'i yul ji lta ba de 'dra ba ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnams la yang ma mchis so//

20a7(mdo sde): su byas shing / lag pa thal mo sbyar nas/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang po la chos kyi rnams grangs 'di nyid mnyan to//

20b1(mdo sde): de bzhin gshegs pa bcu gnyis gshegs nas/ rigs kyi bu ma 'jigs shig/ khyed kyis theg pa chen po'i mdo sde'i rgyal po za ma tog bkod pa thos so// bde ba
20b2(mdo sde): can du 'gro ba'i phyir lam sna tshogs kyang sta gon byaso// gdugs sna tshogs dang / cod pan dang / rna cha dang / se me do'i rnams kyang sta gon byas so zhes dbugs 'byin
20b3(mdo sde): par mdzad de/ ltas de lta ba 'byung zhing / 'chi ba'i dus kyi che bar chad med par bde ba can du 'gro bar 'gyur ro// lag na rin po che de ltar byang chub sems dpa' sngun ras
20b4(mdo sde): gzigs kyi dbang po de ni/ lha ma yin rnams la mya ngan las 'da' ba'i sa ston par byed/ sgo ston par byed do// de nas byang chub sems dpa' lag na rin po tshos

20b8(mdo sde): pa smra bar 'gyur te/ de'i tshe de'i dus su ngas de bzhin gshegs pa las/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang po'i yon tan
21a1(mdo sde): #rjod pa thos te/ 'di lta ste gser gyi sa la song nas/ sems can spri'u tshugs su 'dug pa rnams la/ 'phags pa'i lam yan
21a2(mdo sde): lag brgyad pa'i lam mya ngan las 'dra bar ston par byed pa dang ldan pa'i chos ston to// de nas gser gyi las byung ste/ dngul gyi sa las song nas/ de nas skyes bu gang zag
21a3(mdo sde): rkang pa bzhi yod pa de dag la/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po spyan ras gzigs dbang po// khyed cag bsam pa dam pa rab kyis mya ngan las 'dra ba'i
