85a5(mdo sde): bya ba dang / snyen bkur bya ba'i phyir nye bar mi 'gro'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ rgyal po gling ldan gyi rgyal po'i pho brang 'khor gyi mi rnams bde ba dang ldan pa'i phyir lta ba dang phyag bya ba dang snyen bkur
85a6(mdo sde): bya ba'i phyir nye bar nye bar mi 'gro'o// kun dga' bo de nas de bzhin gshegs pa mar me mdzad 'di snyam du rgongs te rgyal po gling ldan gyi rgyal po'i pho brang khor gyi rnams rje ba dang ldan
85a7(mdo sde): pas ha nang bag med par gyur gyis ngas de rnams chung zhig yid dbyung bar bya gor chag snyam mo de nas de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas mar me mdzad kyis
85a8(mdo sde): de'i tshe 'di lta bu'i rdzu 'phrul mngon par 'du mdzad pa la mngon par 'du mdzad do// rdzu 'phrul ji lta bu mngon par 'du mdzad pa mngon par 'du mdzad pas rgyal po gling ldan gyi rgyal po'i pho brang 'khor ba'i
85b1(mdo sde): mi rnams kyi nang du bai dUr+ya las byas pa'i grong khyer chen po lta na sdug pa skye bo dang mi mang pos gang ba/ mi de dag kyang lhag par mdzes pa lhag par lta na sdug pa/ rgyan thams cad kyis brgyan pa
85b2(mdo sde): dag cig mngon par sprul to// de nas rgyal po gling ldan gyis rgyal po'i pho brang 'khor ba'i mi rnams bai du r+ya las byas pa'i grong khyer na gnas pa'i mi rnams kyis spa gong bar ni gyur na gang yang
85b3(mdo sde): skyo bar ma gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sa pa'i sangs rgyas mar me mdzad 'di snyam du rgongs te/ rgyal po gling ldan gyi rgyal po'i
85b4(mdo sde): pho bra nga' khor ba'i mi rnams ha rang bag med pa dang ldan par gyur pas/ ngas yang chung zad cig skyo ba skyed par gor ma chag snyam mo// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag
85b5(mdo sde): papar rdzogs sangs rgyas mar me mdzad kyis yang 'di lta bu'i rdzu 'phrul mngon par 'du mdzad pa mngon par 'du mdzad de/ rdzu 'phrul ji lta bu mngon par 'du mdzad pa mngon par 'du mdzad pas//
85b6(mdo sde): bai dur+ya las byas pa'i grong khyer chen po de la me chen po 'bar bar byin gyis brlabs so// byin gyis brlabs ma thag tu de la me bar bar gyur to// de nas de'i tshe sems can de dang / grong khyer
85b7(mdo sde): chen po de yang yongs su zad cing mthar thug pa dang / zhig par gyur nas sems can de dag kyang tshul ma yin pas sdug bsngal bar gyur to// kun dga' bo de nas rgyal po gling ldan gyi rgyal po
85b8(mdo sde): pho brang 'khor ba'i mi rnams kyi bai du ru las byas pa'i grong khyer chen po rgud par mthong nas/ sngangs skrag cing skyo bar gyur nas spu zing zhes byed de/ de dag 'di snyam du sems par gyur te/
86a1(mdo sde): gang gi phyir grong khyer de yongs su zad cing mthar thug pa dang / zhig par gyur pa lags na/ ring po mi thogs par bdag cag kyang de lta bu'i mi rtag pa'i gnas skabs su 'gyur na su zhig
86a2(mdo sde): bdag cag gi skabs su 'gyur snyam mo// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas mar me mdzad 'di snyam du dgongs te/ rgyal po gling ldan gyi rgyal po'i pho brang 'khor
86a3(mdo sde): ba'i mi 'di rnams yongs su smin pas/ ngas chos ston pa kun shes pas nu shing skal pa dang ldan pa dang / mthu yod par gyur to snyam mo// de bzhin gshegs pa mar me mdzad kyis mi de rnams kyi bsam pa
86a4(mdo sde): thugs su chud nas/ de'i tshe dran pa dang shes bzhin gyis/ byang chub kyi snying po de nas bzhengs te/ phyi bzhin 'brang ba'i dge sbyong lha'i dbang po brgya byin dang thabs gcig tu rgyal po'i pho brang ga la ba der
86a5(mdo sde): gshegs so// kun dga' bo de bzhin gshegs pa mar me mdzad byon ma thag tu/ de nas de'i tshe de bzhin gshegs pa mar me mdzad kyis chos ston pa dang po'i tshe srog chags nye khri rab tu phyung ste/ de dag this
86a6(mdo sde): cad rab tu len pa med par zag pa rnams las sems rnam par grol lo// chos snyan pa gnyis kyis de'i tshe srogs chags sum khri rab tu phyung ste/ de dag kyang len pa med par zag pa rnams las sems
86a7(mdo sde): rnam par grol lo// chos bstan pa gsum pa'i tshe srog chags bzhi khri rab tu byung ste/ de dag thams cad chos rnams la chos kyi mig rdul med cing dri ma dang bral ba rnam par dag go/ chos bstan pa bzhi pa'i
86a8(mdo sde): che srogs chags lnga khri rab tu phyung ste/ de dag thams cad len pa med par zag pa las sems rnam par grol lo// kun dga' bo de nas de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sang+yas
86b1(mdo sde): mar me mdzad dge slong gi 'dage 'dun mang pos yongs su skor cing mdun gyis ltas te chos ston to// kun dga' bo de nas rgyal po ma skyes sgras rgyal po gling ldan gyi bu zhig des bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs
86b2(mdo sde): pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas so// zhes thos nas pho nya btang ste/ 'di ltar bdag kyang mchod pa tshal na bdag gi thad du gshegs par gsol zhes spring ngo // de nas pho nya des rgyal po
86b3(mdo sde): ma skyes dgra las gnyan nas/ rgyal po gling ldan gyi rgyal po'i pho brang ga la ba dang / rgyal po gling ldan ga la ba der song ste phyin nas/ 'phrin de skad smras so// de nas rgyal po gling ldan de bzhin gshegs
86b4(mdo sde): pa dgra bcom pa drag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas mar me mdzad ga la ba der song ste phyin nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyis zhabs la mgo bos phyag 'tshal te/ phyogs gcig tu 'dug nas skabs de gsol
86b5(mdo sde): ba dang / bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rgyal po chen po khyod snying las chung ngur gyis la slar song shig/ nga ni rgyal po'i pho brang pad ma can du gshegs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bco
86b6(mdo sde): pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas mar me mdzad dge slong gi dge 'dun dang / byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs dang / lha dang klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang lha ma yin dang / na mkha' lding dang mi'i
86b7(mdo sde): ci dang lto 'phye chen po dang / mi dang mi yin pa rnams kyis yongs su skor cing / rgyal po gling ldan yang rgyal po'i mthu chen po dang / rgyal po'i tshogs tshogs mang po dang / rgyal po'i rnam par 'phrul pa chen
86b8(mdo sde): po dang / rgyal po'i bdog pa chen po dang / rgyal po'i 'byor pa chen po dang / rgyal po'i rnam par rtse ba chen po dang chas te/ yongs su skor cing mdun gyis ltas te/ thabs gcig tu gshegs so//
87a1(mdo sde): kun dga' bo de nas de bzhin gshegs pa mar me mdzad de rim gyis rgyal po'i pho brang pad ma can ga la ba der gshegs so// de'i tshe na ri'i rgyal po gangs ri la bram ze rin
87a2(mdo sde): po che zhes bya ba zhig 'dug ste/ bram ze'i khye'u lnga brgya tsam stan chos dang / rigs byed dang / gsang sngags thams cad slob tu 'jug go// de na bram ze'i khye'u lnga brgya tsam po de dag gi nang
87a3(mdo sde): na bram ze'i khye'u sprin ces bya ba gzho nu dar la babs pa/ gzugs bzang ba mdzes pa lta na sdug pa/ kha dog bzang po rgyas pa/ mchog dang ldan pa/ bsang sngags dang stan chos dang / cho ga shes
87a4(mdo sde): pa ji snyed pa thams cad la mkhas pa zhig yod do// kun dga' bo de nas bram ze'i khye'u sprin ces bya bas mkhan po'i rkang pa la mgo bos phyag 'tshal nas 'di skad ces smras so// kye mkhan po bdag
87a5(mdo sde): grong dang grong khyer dang / ljongs dang / yul 'khor dang / rgyal po'i pho brang 'khor rnams su mchi'o// mkhan pos smras pa/ kye bram ze'i khye'u bdag cag bram ze rnams kyi chos nyid ni 'di yino//
87a6(mdo sde): gang gis stan bcos dang / rig byed dang / bsang sngags thams cad lobs pa des mkhan po la zong brgya dang / ras zum gcig dang / khar ba dang ril ba rnams sbyin dgos so// bram ze'i
87a7(mdo sde): khyi'u sprin gyis smras pa/ mkhan po bdag la pags pa dang / khar ba dang ril pa ma gtogs par ci yang ma mchis pas mchi'o// lan gsum gyi bar du gsol nas/ de bzhin gyis
87a8(mdo sde): shig ces smras so// de nas bram ze'i khye'u sprin rim gyis ri'i rgyal po gangs la babs nas/ grong dang grong khyer dang / ljongs dang / yul 'khor dang / rgyal po'i pho brang 'khor du zhug so//
87b1(mdo sde): de'i tshe na grong khyer chen po bde bar pha rol tu 'gro ba na bram ze sa ga bzang po zhes bya ba zhig gnas te/ de la bu mo bzang len ldan bya ba gzugs bzad pa mdzes pa/ lta na sdug pa/ kha dog bzang po
87b2(mdo sde): rgyal po mchog dang ldan pa zhig yod pa de'i phyir nyi ma re re zhing bram ze bzhi khri zan sbyin par byed cing / de rnams nang nas thams cad las khyed par du 'phags pa yin pa de la bdag gis bu bo sbyin
87b3(mdo sde): no snyam pa dang / gnas gtsang ma'i ris kyi lha'i bu zhig gis bram ze'i khye'u sprin la grong khyer chen po bde bar pha rol tu 'gro ba'i lam ston to// de nas ze'i khye'u sprin mchod sbyin gyi gnas ga
87b4(mdo sde): la ba der song ste phyin to// bram ze'i khye'u sprin mchod sbyin gyi gnas der phyin ma thag tu de'i tshe bu mo des rang gi pha ma la 'di skad ces smras so// yab bram ze'i khye'u 'di'i mtshan ma ji ltar gdar
87b5(mdo sde): ba la sa ni 'di bdag gi khyim thab du 'gyur ro// de nas bram ze'i khye'u sprin bram ze de dag thams cad dang / lhan cig kun tu smra bar byed cing / de na bram ze sprin nyid stan bcos dang / gsang sngags
87b6(mdo sde): ngag gis khyed par du 'phags so// de'i tshe na mchod sbyin gyi gnas der bram ze dum bu byin zhes bya ba zhib rgan gral du 'dug ste mdo sbyin byed do// de nas bram ze'i khye'u sprin bram ze dum bu byin
87b7(mdo sde): ga lA ba der song ste phyin nas/ bram ze dum bu sbyin dang lhan cig tu rig byed dang gsang sngags dag smra bar byed cing / de na 'di lta ste sprin nyid rig byed dang gsang sngags dang / stan ces bdag
87b8(mdo sde): gis khyad par du 'phags so// de nas bram ze'i khye'u sprin gyis/ bram ze dum bu sbyin la 'di skad ces smras so// kye bram za bdag cag bram ze rnams kyi chos nyid ni gang gis stan cos papa
88a1(mdo sde): cad rtogs shing khong du chud pa de stan mchog la 'dug pa yin no// de nas bram ze'i khye'u sprin gyi dum bu byin la 'di skad ces smras so// bram ze chen po 'dir kho bo 'dug
88a2(mdo sde): gis stan 'di las longs shig/ de nas bram ze dum bu byin gyis/ 'di skad ces smras so// bram ze'i khye'u kho bo stan 'di las ma bslangs shig dang / kho bo zong lnga brgya thob pa khyod la
88a3(mdo sde): byin no// smras pa khyo bo la mi rgos so// de ma langs pa dang / de'i 'grin pa nas bzung ste bslang ngo // de nas bram ze dum bu byini byas/ bram ze khye'u sprin la smras pa/ bram ze'i khye'u khyod kyis
88a4(mdo sde): kho bo stan 'di las slang nas the brtsams shing sngangs par byas pas/ khyod gang dang gang du skyes pa'i skyes pa thams cad du sbyin pa'i bar chad bya'o// zhes dam bcas so// de nas bram ze'i
88a5(mdo sde): khye'u spyan seng ge'i khri de la 'dug go/ de nas bram ze sa ga bzang pos bu mo bzang len ldan lag pa g.yas pas bzung ste/ gser gyi khar ba dang ril pa dang / ras zung cig dang / zong lnga
88a6(mdo sde): brgya khyer nas/ bram ze'i khye'u ga la ba der song ste phyin nas/ bram ze'i khye'u sprin la 'di skad ces smras so// rigs kyi bu 'di dag long shig/ de nas bram ze'i khye'u sprin gyis zong lnga

88a8(mdo sde): 'phyar ba/ dge ba'i bar cad byed pa yin la/ kho bo ni dgon pa rab tu dben pa rnams na gnas pas 'di kho bo la mi dgos so// rigs kyi bu bdag la snying rtse ba'i phyir long shig des ma blangaso//
88b1(mdo sde): de nas bram ze'i khye'u sprin mchod sbyin gnas de nas song ste/ ri'i rgyal po gangs ga la ba der song ngo // de nas bram ze sa ga bzang po des bu mo bzang len ldan la smras pa/ bu mo khyod khyim thab

88b3(mdo sde): su 'gro ba'i lam mi snang bar byas nas/ rgyal po'i pho brang pad ma can du gang nas 'gro ba'i lam snyan cing / gang du bram ze'i khyi'u sprin dro 'debs pa der bu mo bzang len ldan yang dgongs 'deb so// /

88b5(mdo sde): brgyan par gyur/ de nas rgyal po'i pho brang 'khor ba'i mi rnams kyi bram ze'i khye'u sprin la 'di skad ces smras so// bram ze'i khye'u khyed kyis ma thos sam/ 'di ltar de bzhin gshegs

88b7(mdo sde): de nas bram ze'i khye'u sprin 'di snyam du sems te/ bdag cag bram ze rnams kyis nang na/ gang stan chos thams cad la spyod pa gsal zhing mkhas pa yang dkon na/ sems can rin po che 'di
88b8(mdo sde): lta bu 'jig rten du byung ba lha mos kyang ci dgos kyis/ bdag gis zong brgya po 'dis me tog nyos la de bzhin gshegs pa la mchod pa bya gor ma chags snyam nas/ des phan tshun me tog btsal
89a1(mdo sde): na gang nas kyang ma rnyed pa dang / rgyal po'i pho brang bar ma can gyi rgyal po'i pho brang 'khor ba'i mi rnams na re bram ze khye'u khyod kyis ma mthos sam/ rgyal po ma skyes
89a2(mdo sde): dgras bka' stsal pa/ me tog thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa mar me mdzad la mchod pa bya dgos kyis/ 'di ltar su yang me tog nyor mi gnang / 'tshong du yang mi gnang ngo // gang
89a3(mdo sde): zhig gis nyos sem btsongs na ngas de chad pa chen pos bcad do zhe'o// me tog tshol bA na bu mo bzang len ldan 'dun du 'dug ste/ 'di skad ces smras so// bram ze'i khye'u ci tshol//
89a4(mdo sde): bram ze'i khye'u sprin gyis smras pa/ bu mo me tog tshol lo// de nas bu mo bu ma bzang len ldan me tog 'phreng rgyud mkhan zhig gi khyim ga la ba der song ste phyin nas/ me tog 'phreng rgyud
89a5(mdo sde): mkhan de la 'di skad ces smras so// rigs kyi bu kho mo la me tog byin cig/ kho mo'i khyim thabs la 'dogs so// me tog 'phreng rgyud mkhan gyis smras pa/ bu mo khyod kyis ma thos sam/
89a6(mdo sde): 'di ltar rgyal po ma skyes dgras 'di skad bka' stsal te/ me tog thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa mar me mdzad la mchod pa bya dgos kyis/ 'di ltar me tog 'tsheng du yang mi gnang / nyer mi
89a7(mdo sde): gnang ngo gang zhig nyos sam/ btsongs na ngas de chang pa chen pos bcod do zhe'o// lan gsum gyi bar du spangs pa dang / de bzhin bya'o zhes zer ba ro// de nas bu bzang len ldan gyis bum
89a8(mdo sde): pa blangs nas/ ud pa la bdun bcug ste/ grong khyer du song nas bram ze'i khye'u sprin mthong ba dang / mdun du 'dug ste 'di skad ces smras so// bram ze'i khye'u ci tshol bu me tog tshol lo//
89b1(mdo sde): smras pa bram ze'i khye'u ci bya smras pa/ bu mo skyed par bya'o// bu mos smras pa/ ud pa la btogs zin pa gang dag yang skye bar 'gyur ba ni kho mos nam yang mthos ma mthong ngo // smras pa/
89b2(mdo sde): bu mo gang la skyed pa tsam gyis skye ba'i bsod nams kyi zhing de lta bu la snyed do// des smras pa/ gal te kho mo gang dang gang du skyes pa'i skyes pa thams cad du kho mo'i khyim thab du 'gyur bar dam
89b3(mdo sde): bca' na/ de'i phyir ud pa la sbyin no// de nas bram ze'i khye'u sprin 'di snyam du sems te/ bdag ni dgon pa dang rab tu dben pa na gnas pa yin la/ bud med ni rgod pa dang / 'phyar ba dge ba'i
89b4(mdo sde): bar chad byed pa yin pas/ bud med 'dis ci zhig bya snyam mo// lan bdun gyi bar du smras pa dang / de bzhin du gyur cig ces smras so// de nas de'i tshe bcom ldan 'das kyis tshigs su
89b5(mdo sde): bcad pa 'di dag bka' stsal to// 'di skad ngas sngon thos srid na// sangs rgyas mar me mdzad 'jig rten 'byung // 'khor ni mang po bdun stong dang // pad ma can du de byon to// de'i phyir
89b6(mdo sde): ni rgyal mtshan bsgreng // rnga ni brgya phrag de phyir bdungs// grong khyer thams cad kun sbyangs shing // lam srang bzhi ni de phyir brgyan// grong khyer brgyan pa de mthong nas// bram ze'i khye'u
89b7(mdo sde): gyis dris pa ni// gang gi phyir ni rgyal mtshan bsgrengs// gang phyir rnga ni brgya phrag bdungs// grong khyer thams cad kun sbyangs shing // gang zhig lam srang bzhi brgyan pa'o// bsam
89b8(mdo sde): bde ni lung ston cig/ rig byed shes khyod ma thos sam// sangs rgyas mar me 'jig rten 'byung // 'khor ni mang po bdun stong dang // pad ma can du de byon te// de phyir rnga ni brgya phrag phus/
90a1(mdo sde): grong khyer thams cad kun sbyangs shing // de phyir lam srang bzhi brgyan to// sangs rgyas kyi ni sgra thos nas/ sangs rgyas yon tan gyis 'gu ste// rings par myur du song ba dang /
90a2(mdo sde): rgyan dang bram ze'i bu mo mthong // pad ma ud pal g.yon pa'i mig/ chu skyes thogs shing sgo na 'dug/ de yis bram ze'i khye'u mthong nas// snyan pas smra bar bya ba'i phyir// ka la bying karma bya'i sgra//
90a3(mdo sde): yi 'ong dang mo khwa byug sgra// sgra chen spangs nas tshangs pa'i sgras// bram ze'i khye'u la bu mos smras pa// khye'u ci nags kyi nang den// sbyin sreg byed cing rig 'dod la// rgyal po'i drimig gis
90a4(mdo sde): ma rtses sam// 'khrug cing lam srang dag tu rgyu// bu mo nga khyim gnyen bdun med// yongs su bzung ba 'drang la med// 'dod pa'i yon tan nga mi 'dod// bu mo rgyal dmag nga mi gnod//
90a5(mdo sde): nga de dag las zan mi za// chos gos gos kyang mi len te// shes bzhin rdzun ni mi sman// bu mo rgyal dmag nga mi gnod// 'bras bu rtsa ba nags na gnas// bu mo rgyal dmag nga mi gnod//
90a6(mdo sde): seng phrag dag gis ma rtses sam// 'bras bu rtsa nags na med dam ci// ci phyir khyod ni rtang par 'os// seng ge phrug gus ma rtses te// nags na 'bras bu rtsa ba yod// bzang mo ud pal
90a7(mdo sde): rgos pa'i phyir// de phyir nga 'dir gong khyer 'ongs// gal te shed pu 25 lang co yis// dregs lus rgyan phyir bram ze'i khye'u// bdag gi ud pa la 'tsham pa yin// bdag gi 'phreng
90a8(mdo sde): phyir mi nyo la// u pal snam phyir 'dod pa min// rtse ldan mar me mdzad kyi phyir// bzang mo dag ni ud pa la song // bde bar pha rol 'gro ba na// gang du pa las zan zon tshe// brlang
90b1(mdo sde): ba'i tshigs smras mi dran nas// 'dzem med ci'i phyir me tog slong // bzang mo ud pal nir du dbyig/ lnga brgya 'di sbyin dge sa mas gnong // sangs rgyas yon tan tshol ba la// bzang
90b2(mdo sde): mo dgegs ni ma byed cig/ bzang mo bdag gi bzhis byas nas// slong ba rnams kyi dgegs su 'gyur// gzhan lta zhog gi/ bram ze'i khye'u// gal te slong la bdag byin na// bdag ni khyod
90b3(mdo sde): kyi dgegs mi byed// bdag smon 'dir 'gyur gzhan du min// bram ze'i khye'us ud pa la blangs// de dag ud pa la thogs nas kyang // rgyal ba'i zhabs la phyag 'tshal nas// ga la
90b4(mdo sde): te bdag lus skams gyur cing // bdag gis rus pa dkar gyur kyang // byang chub lung ma snyan par du// bdag ni de ring mi ldang ngo // bdag smon der gyur gzhan du min// de nas bu mo len
90b5(mdo sde): ldan gyis ud pa la lnga blangs te// bram ze'i khye'u sprin la byin nas// bram ze'i khye'u ud pa la 'di dag rang gi ming gis skan cig/ bram ze'i khye'u ud pa la 'di gnyis kyang kho me'i ming
90b6(mdo sde): gyis skan cig/ de nas bram ze'i khye'u sprin ud pa la de dag khyer nas grong khyer gyi phyi rol tu byung ba dang de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas mar me mdzad
90b7(mdo sde): mdzes pa dad par bya ba dbang po dul ba// thugs dul ba/ mchog tu dul ba/ dang zhing zhi ba'i pha rol tu phyin pa/ dul ba dang zhi ba dang dam pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa glang po chen po// dbang

91a3(mdo sde): la mchod pa'i phyir 'ong ba yang mthong nas/ yang 'di snyam du sems par gyur to// de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas ni skyes bu chen po'i mtshan

91a5(mdo sde): cu zhig snang ste/ mtshan gnyis ni mi snang bas/ mtshan sum cu gnyis dang ldan pa ma yin no// snyam mo// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dag bcom pa yang dag
91a6(mdo sde): par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas mar mdzad kyis/ bram ze'i khye'u sprin gyi sems kyis kun tu rtog pa thugs su chud nas/ rdzu 'phrul ji lta bu mngon par 'du mdzad mngon par 'du mdzad pas/

91b2(mdo sde): kyis dpags pa brtsogs pa 'di gding bar byed/ de nas bram ze'i khye'u sprin gyis dpags pa blangs nas las bzur te/ lam gol bar 'dug nas bden pa'i tshigs 'di byas so//

91b6(mdo sde): byas pa'i ral pa yin pa'i phyir ro// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas mar me mdzad shul la bzur nas bram ze'i khye'u sprin gang na

92a1(mdo sde): bzhi ka ba ba zhig/ cha mnyam pa shin tu rnam par phye ba/ nyam dga' ba yid du 'ongs pa zhig gnas par gyur te/ khang partsegs pa de yang de bzhin gshegs
92a2(mdo sde): pa'i sku snang ngo // de nas de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas mar me mdzad kyis bram ze'i khye'u sprin la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// bram ze'i

92a8(mdo sde): ba dang / dge slong gi dngos po gsol to// kun dga' bo de'i tshe de'i dus na bram ze'i khri'u sprin ces bya ba gyur pa de gzhan zhig yin snyam du sem nyi'am// yid gnyis sam/ the tsom zan/
92b1(mdo sde): kun dga' bo de de ltar mi lta'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ nga nyid de'i tshe de'i dus na bram ze'i khye'u sprin ces bya ba der gyur to// kun dga' bo de'i tshe de'i dus na bram ze'i bu mo bzang len ldan

96b5(mdo sde): zhabs bring du 'brang ngo // de nas lha'i dbang po brgya byin las stsogs pa sum bcu rtsa gsum gyi lha rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das them skas su zhugs par rig nas/ bcom ldan 'das la mchod
96b6(mdo sde): pa'i las kyi phyir lha'i spos kyi sprin gyi char rab tu phab ste/ thal mo sbar bcom ldan 'das la mngon par bstod pa/ rdzu 'phrul dam pa brnyes shing rab tu tshangs pa med pa rnam par 'phrul pa shin
96b7(mdo sde): tu sten/ rgyal ba nyi ma ji bzhin 'phags te/ zhing rnams bye ba brgya dag tu yang rab tu gda'/ rgyal bas rang gis yon tan kun gyis zhing rnams thams cad brgyan te shin tu mdzes mdzad pa/
96b8(mdo sde): gang zhig shin tu mnyam med mtshungs pa med cing rdzu 'phrul dbang du gyur pa la phyag 'tshal lo// de nas sum bcu rtsa gsum gyi lha rnams kyis bcom ldan la tshigs su bcad pa 'dis mngon
97a1(mdo sde): @par bstod nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyis zhabs bring du 'brang ngo // de nas lha'i rgyal po rab mtshe ma las stsogs pa mtshe ma'i lha rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das
97a2(mdo sde): them skas su bzhugs par rig nas/ bcom ldan 'das la mchod pa'i las kyi phyir lha'i na bza'i sprin gyi char rab tu phab te/ thal mo sbar nas bcom ldan 'das la mngon par bstod pa/
97a3(mdo sde): bder gshegs khyod kyis mkhyen pa mtha' yas yangs pas sems can bsam pa mkhyen// mkha' 'dra'i lam gyi dus sum dag la chags med thams cad mkhyen pa nyid// sems
97a4(mdo sde): dkyis 'jug pa gcig gi 'gro ba'i sems kyi spyod pa thams cad mkhyen// des na srid pa gsum po dag na lus can rnams kyis mchod par 'os// de nas mtshe ma'i lha rnams kyis bcom

97a6(mdo sde): ldan gyi lha rnams kyi sa bcom ldan 'das them skas su zhugs pa rigs nas/ bcom ldan 'das la mchod pa'i las kyi phyir lha'i rin po che'i sprin gyis char rab tu phab ste/ thal
97a7(mdo sde): mi sbyar nas bcom ldan 'das la mngon par bstod pa/ gang gi slad du sgra dang yi ge ma mchis gang du'ang rgyu ba ma mchis pas/ khyod kyi chos rnams g.yo ba ma mchis dbang gyur sgyu ma
97a8(mdo sde): smig rgyu sgyu ma 'drar mkhyen nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyis thugs rjes sems can rnams la ched du chos mchog gsungs pas na/ chos kyi dngos po'i rang bzhin mkhas pa bdag med
97b1(mdo sde): gsung ba'i rgyal la phyag 'tshal lo// de nas dga' ldan gyi lha rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das la tshigs su bcad pa 'dis mngon par bstod nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyis zham ring du 'brang ngo //
97b2(mdo sde): de nas lha'i rgyal po rab 'phrul las stsogs pa 'phrul dga'i lha rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das them skas su zhugs par rig nas/ bcom ldan 'das la mchod pa'i las kyi phyir lha'i rgyan gyi
97b3(mdo sde): sprin gyi char rab tu phab ste/ thal mo sbyar nas bcom ldan 'das la tshig su bcad nas 'dis mngon par bstod pa// chos kyi zong gis rang gi stobs bcu'i mkha' 'dra 'od zer ldan pa dang /
97b4(mdo sde): thugs rjes brnyes nas byams pa'i dgongs pas sems can rnams la gzugs ston pa// gru tshul chos la gnyis su med par zhugs kyang rgyal ba mtshungs par mkhyen// chos kyi khyad par sems
97b5(mdo sde): lhag don kun grub pa'i rgyal la phyag 'tshal lo// de nas 'phrul dga'i lha rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das la tshigs su bcad pa 'dis par bstod nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyis zham ring du 'brang bar
97b6(mdo sde): gyur to// de nas rgyal po dbang sgyur las stsogs pa/ gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyis lha rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das them skas su zhugs pa dang / 'khor gyi khyams su mngon par phyogs par
97b7(mdo sde): rig nas/ bcom ldan 'das la mchod pa'i las bya ba'i phyir/ mu tig gi do shal gyi sa sprin gyi char rab tu phab ste/ thal mo sbyar nas/ bcom ldan 'das la tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag gis
97b8(mdo sde): mngon par bstod to// tshul khrims dri ma mi mnga' rnam par ngas pa dam pa ting nge 'dzin mchog mi g.yos// mnyam med blo ldan rgya mtsho 'dra bar gnas shing srid las rnam grol dbang sgyur zhabs
99a1(mdo sde): la phyag 'tshal lo// rims kyi byams dang ldan pa'i thugs rjes yis ni bde ba'i lam gyi rnams la rab tu gnas pa mdzad pa/ rnam thar gsum gyi lam gyi khyim na gnas pa'i bder
99a2(mdo sde): gshegs seng ge khyod la bdag cag phyag 'tshal lo// snying rje'i chu bo ting nge 'dzin gyis rnam 'phel ba// zhi gnas 'dab ma rnams par grol pa'i me tog rgyas// slob ma'i tshogs kyi bud bas nges par
99a3(mdo sde): brnyer gyur pa// bder gshegs pad ma la ni spyi bos phyag 'tshal lo// mnga' bdag g.yo ba ma mchis tshul khrims sar gnas pa// brtson 'grus mtshungs pa ma mchis stobs kyis yang dag
99a4(mdo sde): 'phags// yul gyi rlung rnams langs pa chen pos mi g.yos pas// sangs rgyas ri bo dam pa khyod la phyag 'tshal lo// mnga' bdag thugs rjes dbyangs kyi dkyil 'khor rnam dag pa// blo
99a5(mdo sde): gter blo mchog gis ni rab tu 'joms mdzad pa// sems can brgya dag gis ni mang pos mchod gyur pa// bde gshegs zla ba khyod la bdag cag phyag 'tshal lo// kha ltar zhi ba bzhi pa'i rnam
99a6(mdo sde): par thar pa'i lam gshegs pa// shes rab 'od kyis phyogs bcu'i ngag ni rgyas 'gyengs shing // skye bo mang po mtshungs med pad ma kha 'byed pa// sangs rgyas nyi ma dam pa khyod la phyag 'tshalo//
99a7(mdo sde): mnga' bdag phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gsum po dag na yang // 'dren pa khyod dang mnyam par dmigs par ma gyur te/ khyod ni yon tan kun gyis yang dag grub par lags// bdag cag khyod la
99a8(mdo sde): stod pas ngoms par 'gyur ma lags// lha dbang klu dang lha ma yin gyis phyogs bgyis pa// lha phyogs brgya dag gis kyang yang dag mngon bstod pa// bsngags pa brgya phrag mang pos yang dag
99b1(mdo sde): mngon par
99b2(mdo sde): mngon pa stod ga/ bde bar gshegs pa bstod 'os khyod la phyag 'tshal lo// de nas gnan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams kyis/ bcom ldan 'das la tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag gis bstod nas
99b3(mdo sde): bcom ldan 'das kyis zham ring du 'brang ngo // de nas bcom ldan 'das de ltar sangs rgyas kyi yul rnam par sprul pa/ tshad med pas lha brgya phrag stong gis mngon par bstod nas// 'khor
99b4(mdo sde): gyi khyams rin po che bkod par gshegs pa de/ ji ltar bcom ldan 'das gling bzhi pa'i 'jig rten gyi khamasi ma mjed 'dir/ them skas na 'khor gyi khyams rin po che bkod par gshegs
99b5(mdo sde): par shes pa de bzhin du stong gsum gyi 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi gling bzhi pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad na yang gshegs par shes so// de nas bcom ldan 'khor gyi khyams stong
99b6(mdo sde): gsum gyis yongs su bzung ba rin po che bkod par gdan seng ge'i khri ji ltar bshams pa la bzhugs so// byang chub sems dpa' dang / nyan thos chen po dag kyang / stan ji rigs pa la
99b7(mdo sde): 'khod par gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das de'i tshe sangs rgyas ting nge 'dzin rnam par thar pa'i sgrib pa med pa la/ sangs rgyas rnam par rol pa zhes bya ba la snyoms par zhugs so// bcom
99b8(mdo sde): ldan 'das sangs rgyas kyi ting nge 'dzin rnam par thar pa sgrib pa med pa la/ sangs rgyas rnam par rol pa zhes bya ba la snyoms par zhugs ma thag tu/ de nas bcom ldan 'das kyi snyi'i spu'i khung bu tham
99b9(mdo sde): cad kyi/ spu'i khung bu re re nas kyang 'od zer gang ga'i klung gi bye ma snyed byung ste/ byung nas kyang shar phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad snang bar byas so// de bzhin du lha dang nub dang //
100a1(mdo sde): byang gi phyogs rnams dang / 'og dang ster dang phyogs mtshams kyi 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad snang bar byas so// 'jig rten gyi khams rnams snang bar byas ma thag tu//
100a2(mdo sde): de nas sems can dmyal ba'i sems can thams cad kyi/ sems can dmyal ba'i sdug bsngal gyi rgyun bcad do// byol song gi skye gnas pa'i sems can rnams la/ gshi rje'i 'jig
100a3(mdo sde): rten pa'i sems can rnams kyi sdug bsngal gyi tshor ba yang rgyun bcad do// sems can thams cad kyang skad cig de la/ 'dod chags kyis gnod par ma gyur cing / zhe sdang gis
100a4(mdo sde): ma yin/ gti mug gi ma yin te/ nyon mongs pa gzhan gyis kyang gnod par ma gyur to// de'i tshe sems can thams cad kyang byams pa'i sems dang / pha lta bu'i 'du shes su gyur to// /

100a6(mdo sde): stobs ni mtha' yas yangs pa brtan pa brtsams gyur te// gang gis brtson 'grus chen po'i stobs kyis bskal pa dag la phyir phyogs spangs// gang gis yon tan dag ni phyogs
100a7(mdo sde): bcu rnams na mthu ldan par brjod pa// shAkya thub pa'i 'od yangs 'gro ba thams cad snang bar byed pa mdzes pa// gang chos rgya chen bla med mnyam pa de de'i zhabs la phyag 'tshal te//
100a8(mdo sde): mkhas pa blo gros ldan pa dag ni bskal pa grangs med rtag tu nyan// blo rgyas gang zhig rdzogs po'i byang chub sems dpa'i bsam pa ji tsam bskyed// thub pa des na gang phyir/
100b1(mdo sde): sems can bde bar zhed pas 'od 'di rlung // mnga' bdag gang zhig brtson 'grus kyis ni bdud stobs mu stegs tshogs bcas pa na mdzad nas// pad ma byung ba bzhin du 'phags shing phyogs
100b2(mdo sde): bcu dag tu ri rab ji bzhin mdzes// gang zhig nyi ma bzhin du snyi'i 'od kyis 'gro ba ma lus snang mdzad pa// de'i chos kyi 'khor lo bzhag pa don chen gsan du rgyal bar gshegs su
100b3(mdo sde): gsol// rab tu bskor bar ma gyur mtshungs pa med par rgyal ba kun gyis bskor bsgyur ba// 'khor lo dam pa stobs bcu sems can thugs brtse ba'i phyir ni de ring bskor bar mdzad//
100b4(mdo sde): srog chags rnams kyis bsten par rnyed bka' legs pa rgya chen de ring 'byung bar 'gyur// gang dag dad pa dang ba che yangs don tu gnyer ba dag de de ring ltos/ de nas 'od zer dag gis sangs rgyas
100b5(mdo sde): kyi zhing thams cad tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag gis go bar byas// byang chub sems dpa' thams cad yang dag par bskul// 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad rab tu g.yo bar byas/ sems
100b6(mdo sde): can thams cad bde bar byas/ nyon mongs pa'i khams thams cad rnam par sbyangs/ mun pa mun nag thams cad gsal/ bdud kyi khyim thams cad mog mog por byas nas/ byang chub sems
100b7(mdo sde): dpa'i 'khor dpag tu med pa dag dang / 'jig rten gyi khams mi mjed du slar 'ongs te/ bcom ldan 'das kyi dbu'i gtsug tu lci bar gyur to// de nas shar phyogs na de bzhin gshegs pa
100b8(mdo sde): dri med rnam dag rin chen 'od byang chub kyi yan lag dang ldan pa'i chos rgyun mi 'chad pa'i 'od zer bkod pa'i rgyal po'o// sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'jig rten gyi khams yon tan mtha' yas
101a1(mdo sde): pa'i rin po che'i bsod nams bkod pas/ rgya che ba dang ldan pa na/ byang chub sems dpa' me tog dpal gyi snying po chos thams cad la dbang bsgyur ba zhes

101a6(mdo sde): kyi yon tan bsngags 'phreng phyogs bcu kun nas brjod// khyod kyi yon tan tshogs mchis zhing gang yon tan gter// der ni chos don gnyer ba bdag cag rab tu mchi//

102a1(mdo sde): gnas rnams kyi mig kyang rnam par sbyong // de nas byang chub sems dpa' de dag gis byang chub sems dpa'i bstod pa tshad med pa/ de dag gis bcom ldan 'das

102b1(mdo sde): mtshungs pa ste// 'gro ba bsam dag bsam pa mnyam nyid yongs su tshim bgyid// sems kyi rgyu dang rnam rtog gang yang mi mnga' yang // sems can bsam pa rnams la rgyal ba dag gis

103a1(mdo sde): can gang dag des rtog pa// de dag skyon med bde zhing rgyab thob par 'gyur/ gang gis ri rab brtsegs pa lta bu'i khrun tsam du// 'jig rten mkhyen pa mtshungs med rgyal
103a2(mdo sde): ba ltas kyang ni// de yis rdzu 'phrul kun gyis stobs kyang brtson 'grus kyi rnam par sprul pas rgyal ba'i spyi gtsug mthong ma nus/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' de dag gis byang chub sems

103a8(mdo sde): dra bas bcom ldan 'das la mngon par bkab ste/ tshigs su bcad pa 'di gnyis kyis bcom ldan 'das la mngon par bstod do// spu'i mtha' dpung ma mchis pa'i zhing 'dzin kyang /
103b1(mdo sde): sems can rnams la mi gnod zhing la mi gnod pas/ mig med rnams kyi rgyal ba'i spyod yul 'tshal bka'/ sangs rgyas sras ni rgyal ba'i byin gyis yang dag 'tshal// zhing gcig
103b2(mdo sde): phyogs la zhing mang rab byams ston mdzad de// kun tu bstan kyang rnam par 'phel dang 'grib ma mchis// bsam pa chen po dag ldan ci 'dar gyur de la// dpag med rdzu 'phrul rnam par sprul
103b3(mdo sde): pas de ston to// de nas byang chub sems dpa' de dag gis// byang chub sems dpa'i bstod pa tshad med pa dag gis// bcom ldan 'das la mngon par bstod nas/ shar dang lho'i/

109b8(mdo sde): mos par byin gyis brlabs so// de nas sangs rgyas kyis mthus byang chub sems dpa' spobs pa'i rgyan bkod pas rab tu zhi ba dang ldan pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin
110a1(mdo sde): la snyoms par zhugs nas/ thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'khor sgri ba lnga rnam par sel bar byin gyis brlabs so// de nas sangs rgyas kyi mthus byang chub sems
110a2(mdo sde): dpa' chos thams cad rnam par 'phrul pa'i rgyal pos brjod pa med par spyod pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ thams cad dang ldan pa 'khor byang chub sems
110a3(mdo sde): dpa' dran zhing de bzhin gshegs pa la dmigs pa mi mjed par byin gyis brlabs so// de nas de'i tshe sangs rgyas kyi mthus byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos dpa' spos zil
110a4(mdo sde): gyis mi non pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin dang snyoms par zhugs nas/ thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'khor bdud dang phyir rgol ba bcom pa byin gyis brlabs so// de nas de'i tshe sangs
110a5(mdo sde): rgyas kyi mthus byang chub sems dpa' bdud rab tu bcom pas bdud kyi dkyil 'khor thams cad rnam par 'dzem pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ byang chub sems
110a6(mdo sde): dpa' bdud rab tu 'jom pa/ bdud kyi dkyil 'khor rnam par 'jom pa'i ting nge 'dzin de la snyoms par zhugs ma thag tu de nas de'i tshe stong gsum gyi stong chen po 'jig rten gyi khams bdud

110b1(mdo sde): stong phrag du mas bcom ldan 'das mchod nas gus pa dang bcas shing zhes dang bcas par thal mo sbar te bcom ldan 'das la gsol ba btab pa/ bcom ldan 'das bdag cag
110b2(mdo sde): gsol 'tshal na/ bcom ldan 'das chos shad du gsol/ bde bar gshegs pa chos bshad du gsol/ byang chub sems dpa' bdud rab tu 'jom pa'i byin gyis brlabs kyis/
110b3(mdo sde): bdag bdud kyi sug las 'dor zhing slan cad sems can rnams la mig dang bral ba'i las mi bgyid do// bcom ldan 'das bdag cag la dbugs 'byung ba stsol cig dang bcom ldan
110b4(mdo sde): 'das kyis thad du mchis te/ bdag cag chos nyan par bgyid do// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis bdud de dag dbugs 'byung ba'i phyir 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// grogs po dag
110b5(mdo sde): legs so legs so// gang gi phyir khyed bdud kyi las kyang 'ong la de bzhin gshegs pa yang chos bshad par gsol ba yang thob shig dang de nyid khyed kyi bdud kyi lam thams cad las

110b7(mdo sde): gcig gis med par 'gyur ro// grogs po dag de bzhin du nyon mongs pa'i mun pa mun nag skal pa brgyar bsags pa yang ye shes kyi stobs sked pa gcig gis med par 'gyur ro// /
110b8(mdo sde): grogs po dag 'di lta ste dper na zla ba'i dkyil 'khor gcig dang / nyi mi'i dkyil 'khor gcig dang nor bu rin po che chen po gcig gas muni pa mun nag thams cad sel to//
111a1(mdo sde): grogs po dag de bzhin du dge ba'i sems lhag mthong dang ldan pa gcig gis mi shes pa'i mun pa mun nag thams cad sel to// grogs po dag de'i phyir khyod dge ba'i
111a2(mdo sde): rtsa ba 'dis rims kyis mis shes pa'i mun pa mun nag thams cad bsal nas/ chos kyi snang ba chen po thog par 'gyur ro// de nas byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi dbang phyug rgyal po chen

111a8(mdo sde): dbang bsgyur ba/ pha rol tu phyin pa thams cad kyi pha rol tu son pa/ thabs la mkhas pa thams cad las nges par skyes pa bdud kyi las dang rtsod pa dang nyon mongs pa thams cad gsal ba/
111b1(mdo sde): pha rol rko ba dang ngan pa'i tshogs can gyi tshogs thams cad rab tu 'dul ba/ tshigs thams cad rab tu dbye ba bstan pa shes pa la mkhas pa/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa chags
111b2(mdo sde): pa ma mchis pa'i pha rol tu son pa/ dran pa dang blo gros dang rtogs pa dang / khrel yod pa dang / mos dang gzugs dang / ye shes rab tu thob pa/ byin gyis brlabs thogs pa ma mchi

111b4(mdo sde): ston pa/ 'khrul pa ma mchis par kha na ma tho ba ma mchis pa'i chos ston pa sems can thams cad kyi sgra dang skad la mkhas pa/ mi 'am ci dang bya ka la bing ka dang / khrung khru gi sgra dang /

112a8(mdo sde): byin dang / tshangs pi 'od mog mog por bgyid pa/ rgya mtsho'i phyag brgya'i ting nge 'dzin rab tu thob pa chos rin po che thams cad yang gzhol ga donon mchog gsum gyi gdung mi bcod pa/
112b1(mdo sde): sems can thams cad yongs su smin par bgyi ba dang / 'dul ba'i cho ga 'tshal ba/ sangs rgyas kyi chos rin po che thams cad kyi mdzod yang dag par 'dzin pa/ sngags pa mtha' yas
112b2(mdo sde): ba dang yang dag par ldan pa bsod nams tshad ma mchis pa bsags pa/ rnam pa'i mchog thams cad dang ldan pa'i thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes la nye bar gyur pa/ phyi ma'i mtha'i
112b3(mdo sde): mA'i skal bar sngags pa mthar mi phyin pa 'di lta bu rnams kyi 'dus pa lags so// bcom ldan 'das de la bdag 'di snyam du bcom ldan 'das ni byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la 'jug
112b4(mdo sde): bas nges par 'byung ba sgrib med pa'i sgo zhes bgyi ba 'dus pa chen po'i le'u'i chos kyi rnam grangs bshad bzhed pa snyam bgyid do// bcom ldan 'das ji tsam du sangs rgyas 'byung ba ni
112b5(mdo sde): phan 'dogs par gyur pa/ sems can thams cad tshim par 'gyur ba/ ma 'ong ba'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba yang dag par bskyed pa/ sems dang po bskyed pa'i byang
112b6(mdo sde): chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bas pa yongs su spong ba/ spyod pa la zhugs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams tshul gcig la 'jug pa phyir mi ldog pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams sangs
112b7(mdo sde): rgyas kyi chos la dbang bskur ba/ skye ba gcig gis thogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rgyu dang / 'bras bu chud mi za ba/ nges pa'i sems can rnams la rkyen nye bar sgrub pa
112b8(mdo sde): ma nges pa'i sems can rnams la snying rje chen po nye bar sgrub pa/ log pa nyid du nges pa'i sems can rnams 'jud pa/ theg pa gsum la mos pa'i sems can rnams la rnam par dgod
113a1(mdo sde): bstan pa ste/ ngo mtshar to// bcom ldan 'das sangs rgyas 'byung ba ni lce dang mi dang lha ma yin du bcas pa'i 'jig rten gyi rgyan lags so// de ci'i slad du zhe na/
113a2(mdo sde): bcom ldan 'das sangs rgyas 'byung bar 'gyur na/ ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba'i chos 'di lta bu 'di dag 'jig rten du 'byung bar 'gyur ro// bcom ldan 'das skyes bu dam pa 'di dag
113a3(mdo sde): gis 'khor gyi khyams 'dir sems skyed pa gcig gis bkod pa gang byin gyis brlabs pa 'di ni nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi skal pa brgya phrag stong du yang ston pa'i

113a7(mdo sde): rang bzhin can gyi mi la la zhig nor bu rin po che bai du ru bor nas/ nor bu 'ching bu la dmigs pa snyam du sems dpa' dang / bcom ldan 'das theg pa chen po bor nas/ nyan thos dang rang
113a8(mdo sde): sangs rgyas kyi theg pa la dmigs par bgyi ba snyam sems pa'i sems can dag ni 'dra ba nyid du bdag la ganga'o// bcom ldan 'das rigs kyi bu'am/ rigs kyi bu me dag sems

113b7(mdo sde): tshogs la len bdun bskor ba byas te/ byang chub sems dpa' gzungs kyi dbang phyug gi rgyal po'i lus lan brgyad brgyad bskor ba byas nas/ byang chub sems dpa'
113b8(mdo sde): gzungs kyi dbang phyug gi rgyal po'i spyi sdug tu snang gyur te// nged des byang chub dpa' gzugs kyi dbang phyug gi rgyal po reg ma thag tu de nas sangs rgyas
114a1(mdo sde): / kyi mthus byang chub sems dpa' gzugs kyi dbang phyug gis rgyal pos thams cad dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs kyi 'od dang seng ge'i khri dang lus brgya

114a8(mdo sde): bstod do// kun tu snang ba kun nas 'od zer can// don rnams lus ston pa kun nas sban// rang byung chos kyi ngo bo nyid la mkhas// bsam gyis mi khyab yon tan dang ldan// skyes/
114b1(mdo sde): bu khyu mchog gis ni 'od zer phyung // zhal yang rnam par spong zhing 'od zer mdzad pa// 'dres pa des ni bdag gi lus la yang // lan brgyar bskor ba bgyis nas spyi bor ni//

116a1(mdo sde): 'di lta bu 'dri bar sems pa ni skyes bu dam pa khyod legs so// de'i phyir rigs kyi bu khyod shin tu legs par nyon la yid la zung shig dang / byang chub sems
116a2(mdo sde): dpa' sems dpa' chen pos ji ltar yon tan 'di dag dang / byang chub sems dpa'i yon tan 'di dag dang / byang chub sems dpa'i yon tan tshad med pa gzhan dag kyang / yongs
116a3(mdo sde): su rdzogs par 'gyur ba dang / myur du chos thams cad la dbang sgyur ba thob par 'gyur ba// ngas khyod la bshad do// byang chub sems dpa' gzungs kyi dbang phyug gi rgyal
116a4(mdo sde): pos/ bcom ldan 'das legs se zhes gsol to// bcom ldan 'das ji ltar nyan pa dang / bcom ldan 'das kyis 'di skad ces kA sngal to// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems
116a5(mdo sde): dpa' rnams kyi rgyan ni bzhi po 'di dag go/ bzhi gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ tshul khrims kyi rgyan dang / ting nge 'dzin gyi rgyan dang / shes rab kyi rgyan dang / gzungs kyi rgyan te/
116a6(mdo sde): rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rgyan bzhi po 'di dag go/ rigs kyi bu de la bang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi tshul khrims kyi rgyan gang zhe na/ rigs kyi bu byang chub
116a7(mdo sde): sems dpa' rnams kyi tshul khrims kyi rgyun ni gcig go// gcig gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ sems can thams cad la gnod pa mi byed pa ste/ byang chub sems dpa' zhe sdang gi sems
116a8(mdo sde): med pa na mams can thams cad med du'o shing dga' ba ste/ rigs kyi bu 'di da byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rgyan gcigag// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' dmas kyisu ma khrims
116b1(mdo sde): kyi rgyan ni gnyis po 'di dag go// gnyis gang zhe na 'di lta ste ngan 'gro'i sgo bcang pa dang / bde 'gro'i sgo 'byed pa ste/ gnyis po 'di dag go// mi ma zung chub sems mam pa rnams
116b2(mdo sde): kyi tshul khrims kyi rgyu ni gsum po 'di dag go// gsum gang zhe na 'ad lnga ste/ lus rnam par dag pa dang ngag rnam par dag pa dang / ji rnam par dag pa ste gsum po 'di dag go// rigs
116b3(mdo sde): kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi tshul khrims kyi rgyan ni gsum po 'di dag go// gsum gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ lus rnam par dag pa dang / ngag rnam par dag pa dang / yid dam
116b4(mdo sde): par dag pa dang / gsum po 'di dag go// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi tshul khrims kyi rgyan ni bzhi po 'di dag go/ bzhi gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ gang 'dod pa de 'byor
116b5(mdo sde): pa dang / gang 'dod pa dang / gang smon pa de yang dag par grub pa dang / gang 'dod pa de thob pa dang / gang rtsom pa de nyams 'og tu chud par byed pa ste/ bzhi po 'di dag ge/ rigs
116b6(mdo sde): kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi tshul khrims kyi rgyan ni lnga po 'di dag go// lnga gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ tshul khrims dang ldan pa'i ting nge 'dzin sgyu med pa yin// shes rab sgyu med
116b7(mdo sde): pa yin/ rnam par grol ba sgyu med pa yin/ rnam par grol ba'i ye shes mthong ba sgyu med pa yin/ yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa chen po bla na med pa sgyu med pa/ yin te lnga po 'di
116b8(mdo sde): dag go/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi tshul khrims kyi rgyan ni drug po 'di dag go// drug gang zhe na 'di ste/ yid la gcags pa med pa'i tshul khrims kyi phyir skyon med pa
117a1(mdo sde): tshul khrims dang / kha na mtho med pa'i tshul khrims kyi phyir nyams pa'i tshul khrims dang / 'dren pa ma yin tshul khrims kyi phyir 'dres pa ma yin pa'i
117a2(mdo sde): tshul khrims dang dge ba'i chos shin tu rim par 'phel ba'i phyir mthun tshams ma yin tshul khrims dang gang gis 'dod par 'gro ba'i tshul khrims kyi phyir rang dga' tshul khrims
117a3(mdo sde): dang / gzhan la rag ma las pa'i shes pas rang gis dbang sbyor ba'i tshul khrims de drug po 'di dag go// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi tshul khrims kyi rgyan ni
117a4(mdo sde): 'di dag go/ bdun gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ tshul khrims dang ldan pa sbyin pa rnam par dag pa dang / bzod pa rnam par dag pa dang / brtson 'grus rnam par dag pa dang / bas
117a5(mdo sde): gtan rnam par dag pa dang / shes rab rnam par dag pa dang / thabs rnam par dag pa dang / bag yod pa rnam par dag pa ste/ bdun po 'di dag go// rigs kyi bu byang
117a6(mdo sde): chub sems dpa' rnams kyi tshul khrims kyi rgyud ni brgyad po 'di dag ge/ brgyad gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ spobs pa phun sum tshogs pa dang / sa phun sum tshogs pa dang /
117a7(mdo sde): rnam bro ba med pa phun sum tshogs pa dang / lhod pa med pa phun sum tshogs pa dang / khon du 'dzin pa med pa phun sum tshogs pa dang / sangs rgyas 'byung ba mnyes par byed
117a8(mdo sde): pa phun sum tshogs pa dang / ngal ba phun sum tshogs pa dang / dge ba shes nyen mgu bar byed pa phun sum tshogs pa ste/ brgyad po 'di dag go// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems
117b1(mdo sde): dpa' rnams kyi tshul khrims kyi rgyan ni dgu po 'di dag go/ dgu po gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ 'jigs pa med par yin/ skrag pa med pa yin/ bsam nges pa yin/ nye bar
117b2(mdo sde): zhi bar yin/ bsil ba yin/ bcings pa lhod pa yin/ sems las su rung ba yin/ sems can shes pa yin/ zhi ba'i sa rjes su thob pa yin te dgu po 'di dag go//
117b3(mdo sde): rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi tshul khrims kyi rgyan ni bcu po 'di dag go/ bcu gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ mtshan dang dpe byed bzang po yongs su rdzogs pa'i
117b4(mdo sde): phyiphyir lus rgyan dang / ji skad smras pa de bzhin byed pa'i phyir ngag gi rgyan dang / nyon mongs pa med pa'i phyir sems kyi rgyan dang / smon lam yongs su rdzogs pa'i phyir zhing
117b5(mdo sde): gi rgyan dang / bsam pa yongs su spong ba'i phyir shes pa'i rgyan dang / can yongs su smin par bya ba'i rgyan dang / sdig pa thams cad mi byed pa'i phyir skye ba'i rgyan dang /
117b6(mdo sde): de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyod pa la rjes su slob pa'i phyir byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i rgyan dang / nga rgyal med pa'i phyir shes pa'i rgyan dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba yongs su sde
117b7(mdo sde): ba'i phyir byang chub kyi snying po'i rgyun dang / tshul khrims kyi rtsa ba la gnas pa mi 'dor ba'i phyir stobs dang mi 'jigs pa'i rgyan dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa'i
117b8(mdo sde): rgyan to/ rigs kyi bu bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi tshul khrims kyi rgyan no// rigs kyi bu de la byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ting nge 'dzin gyi/
118a1(mdo sde): zhe na/
118a2(mdo sde): rgyan dang / rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ting nge 'dzin gyi rgyan gcig go/ gcig gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ sems can thams cad la byams
118a3(mdo sde): pa ste 'di dag ni gcig go/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ting nge 'dzin gyi rgyan gnyis po 'di dag go// gnyis gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ drang ba dang mnyes pa ste// /
118a4(mdo sde): gnyis po 'di dag go/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ting nge 'dzin gyi rgyan ni gsum po 'di dag go/ gsum gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ sgyu med pa dang / g.yo
118a5(mdo sde): med pa dang / bcos pa med pa dang gsum po 'di dag go/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ting nge 'dzin gyi rgyani na bzhi po 'di dag go/ bzhi gang zhe na 'di
118a6(mdo sde): lta ste/ 'dod pas 'gro ba ma yin par mi 'gro ba dang / zhe sdang gis 'gre ba ma yin par mi 'gro ba dang / gti mugi ga 'gro ba ma yin mi 'gro ba dang / 'jigs/
118a7(mdo sde): pa sa 'gro ba ma yin mi 'gro ba ste/ bzhi po 'di dag go/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ting nge 'dzin gyi rgyan ni lnga po 'di dag gi/ lnga gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ sgrib
118a8(mdo sde): ba lnga spong ba'o// lnga gang zhe na 'dod par bya ba la 'dod pa dang / gnod sems dang rmugs pa dang / gnyid dang rgod pa dang / 'gyod pa the tsom ste/ sgri pa lnga po 'di dag spongs pa'o//
118a9(mdo sde): rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ting nge 'dzin gyi rgyan ni drug po 'di dag go/ drug gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa dang / chos rjes su dran pa dang / dge 'dun
118b1(mdo sde): rjes su dran pa dang / gtong ba rjes su dran pa dang / tshul khrims rjes su dran pa dang / lha rjes su dran pa ste/ drug po 'di dag go// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ting nge 'dzin gyi
118b2(mdo sde): rgyan ni bdun po 'di dag go/ bdun gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa'i mi rjed pa'i byang chub kyi yan lag bdun bsgom ste/ dran pa yang dag byang chub kyi yan lag dang / chos
118b3(mdo sde): rab tu 'byed pa yang dag byang chub yan lag dang / brtson 'grus yang dag byang chub kyi yan lag dang / shin tu sbyangs pa yang dag byang chub kyi yan lag dang / ting nge 'dzin yang dag byang
118b4(mdo sde): chub kyi yan lag dang / btang snyoms yang dag byang chub kyi yan lag dang / bdun po 'di dag go// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ting nge 'dzin gyi rgyan ni brgyad po 'di dag go//
118b5(mdo sde): brgyad gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad po sgom pa ste/ 'di ltar yang dag par lta ba dang / yang dag par rtog pa dang / yang dag pa'i ngag dang / yang dag pa
118b6(mdo sde): las kyi mtha' dang / yang dag pa'i mcho ba dang / yang dag pa'i rtsol ba dang / yang dag pa'i dran pa dang / yang dag pa'i ting nge 'dzin te brgyad po 'di dag go// rigs kyi bu byang chub sen
118b7(mdo sde): dpa' rnams kyi ting nge 'dzin gyi rgyan ni dgu po 'di dag go// dgu gang zhe na rigs kyi bu 'di la byang chub sems dpa' brjed pa med pa'i sems kyi snying rje chen po'i gnas la gnas te/
118b8(mdo sde): sems can thams cad yongs su mi gtong bar gnas nas/ 'dod pa rnams la dben pa sdig pa mi dge ba'i chos rnams las dben pa/ rnam par rtog pa bcas pa/ rnam par spyod pa/
119a1(mdo sde): dang bcas pa dben pa las skyes pa'i dga' ba dang / bde ba can bsam gtan dang po rdzogs par byas te gnas so// de rnam par rtog pa dang / rnam par spyod pa
119a2(mdo sde): nye bar zhi ba ste nang shin tu dang zhing sems kyi rgyud gcig tu gyur pas/ rnam par rtog pa med cing / rnam par spyod pa med pa/ ting nge 'dzin las skyes pa dga' ba dang bde ba can/ bsam
119a3(mdo sde): gtan gnyis pa rdzogs par byas te gnas so// dga' ba'i 'dod chags dang bral te/ btang snyoms can du gnas pa la dran pa dang / ldan zhing bshes bzhin gyis bde ba la lus kyi tshor te/
119a4(mdo sde): gang 'phags pa rnams kyis btang snyoms can du dran pa dang ldan zhing bde bar gnas pa'o zhes brjod pa dga' ba med pa'i bsam gtan gsum pa rdzogs par byas te gnas so// de bde
119a5(mdo sde): ba yang spangs sdug bsngal ba yang spangs te bde ba dang / yid mi bde ba snga nas nub pas/ bde ba yang med sdug bsngal ba yang med de btang snyoms dang dran pas yongs su dag pa
119a6(mdo sde): bsam gtan bzhi pa rdzogs par bas te gnas so// de rnam pa thams cad du gzugs kyis 'du shes las shin tu 'das te/ thogs pa'i 'du shes rnams kyi rgyan ni gnyis po 'di byed pa// /
119a7(mdo sde): namakha' mtha' yas so snyam nas/ nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched rdzogs par byas te gnas so// de rnam pa thams cad du na mkha' mtha' yas skye mched las shin tu 'das te/ rnam
119a8(mdo sde): par shes pa mtha' yas so snyam nas/ rnam shes mtha' yos skye mched las 'das par byas ste gnas so// de rnam pa thams cad du rnam shes mtho' yas skye mched las shin tu 'das te/
119b1(mdo sde): cing yang med do snyam nas ci yang med pa'i skye mched rdzogs par byas te gnas so// de rnam pa thams cad du ci'ang med pa'i skye mched las shin tu 'das te/ 'di shin med min skye mched rdzogs
119b2(mdo sde): par byas te gnas so// de rnam pa thams cad 'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched las 'das te/ 'du sheso dang tshor ba dang 'gog pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa la/ snyoms par
119b3(mdo sde): 'jug kyang / thabs mkhas pas yang dag pa'i mtha' mngon sum du 'ong mi byed la/ sngon gyi byin brlabs kyis yang langs nas/ sems can rnams kyang yongs su smin par byed pa ste/
119b4(mdo sde): ting nge 'dzin gyi rgyan ni chu bo 'di dag go// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ting nge 'dzin gyi rgyan ni bcu po 'di dag gi/ bcu gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ mi khrug pas nges par nges
119b5(mdo sde): bor sems pa dang / zhi gnas dngos su rdzogs par byed pa dang / mngon par brtson pa mi 'dor ba dang / nang du yang dag 'jogs sred pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams chud mi za ba dang /
119b6(mdo sde): sems dben pa dang / lus shin tu spungs pa dang / chos rnams la sems shing 'jal la so sor rtogs pa dang / sems la dbang sgyur ba dang / 'phags pa'i rigs rab tu thob pa
119b7(mdo sde): ste/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ting nge 'dzin gyi rgyan ni bcu po 'di dag go/ rigs kyi bu de la byang chub sems dpa'i rnams kyi shes rab kyi rgyan gang zhe na/ rigs kyi bu
119b8(mdo sde): byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi shes rab kyi rgyan ni gcig go// gcig gang zhe na 'di lta ste chos thams cad la the tshom med pa ste/ 'di gcig go// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpal
120a1(mdo sde): smra stsa du gas sa
120a2(mdo sde): kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi shes rab kyi rgyan ni gsum po 'di dag go/ gsum gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ gti mug spong ba dang / ma rigs pa'i sgo nga'i sbubs nges
120a3(mdo sde): bar gcog pa dang / mun pa mun nag sel ba sel ba ste/ gsum po 'di dag go/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi shes rab kyi rgyan ni bzhi po 'di dag go/ bzhi gang
120a4(mdo sde): zhe na 'di lta ste/ sdug bsngal yongs su shes par bya ba'i shes pa dang / kun tu 'byung ba spong ba'i snang ba dang / 'gog pa mngon gsum du bya ba'i 'od dang / lam sgom pa'i byin
120a5(mdo sde): brlabs te bzhi po 'di dag go/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi shes rab kyi rgyan ni 'di dag go// lnga gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ dmigs pa med pas tshul khrims kyi phung
120a6(mdo sde): po yongs su dag pa dang / shes rab mchog gi bsam gtan pa yin pas/ ting nge 'dzin gyi phung po yongs su dag pa dang / gnyis dang bral bas rnam par grol ba'i phung po yongs su
120a7(mdo sde): dag pa dang / dus gsum mnyam pa nyid pas rnam par grol bar ye shes mthong ba'i phung po yongs su dag pa ste/ 'dod chags bral ba'i chos nyid pas chos kyi phung po yongs su
120a8(mdo sde): dag pa ste/ lnga po 'di dag go/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi shes rab kyi rgyan ni drug po 'di dag go// drug gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ 'khor gsum yongs su dag
120b1(mdo sde): kha'i sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa ni/ sgyu ma dang mnyam pa nyid pas bdag gi 'khor yongs su dag pa ste/ mi lam dang mnyam pa nyid pas/ sems can gyi 'khor yongs su dag pa dang /
120b2(mdo sde): rnam par smin pa la re ba med pas byang chub kyi 'khor yongs su dag po// 'khor gsum yongs su dag pa'i tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni/ gzugs rnyan lta bu'i phyir lus kyi
120b3(mdo sde): 'khor yongs su dag pa dang / lta bu'i shes pa gang ga'i 'khor yongs su dag pa dag dang / sgyu ma dang mnyam pa nyid pas sems kyi 'khor yongs su dag pa'o// 'khor
120b4(mdo sde): gsum yongs su dag pa'i bzod pa'i bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa ni nyes par smras pa'i tshig rnams la khro khro ba spong ba yongs su dag pa'o// bstod pa dang sngags pa dang / rjes
120b5(mdo sde): su 'chags pa yongs su dag pa dang / yan lag dang nyin lag gcod pa dag la chos kyi ska la rab tu rtog pa yongs su dag pa'o// 'khor gsum yongs su dag pa'i brtson 'grus kyi pha rol
120b6(mdo sde): tu phyin pa ni 'khor ba rmi lam lta bur mos pas yongs su mi skyo ba yongs su dag pa dang / rdo rje lta bu'i bsam gtan yongasu dag pa dang / mtshan ma thams cad las grol bas blang ba med dang /
120b7(mdo sde): dor ba med pa yongs su dag pa'o// 'khor gsum yongs su dag pa'i bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni 'gyur shes pas de la ma chags pa yongs su dag pa dang / mngon par shes
120b8(mdo sde): pa med pas/ lhag mthong yongs su dag pa dang / mngon par shes pa skyed pa'i dmigs pas yongs su dag pa'o// 'khor gsum yongs su dag pa'i thabs kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni//
121a1(mdo sde): sems can yongs su smin par byed pas/ bsdu ba'i dngos po yongs su dag pa dang / dam pa'i chos yongs su 'dzin pas gzungs yong su dag pa dang / sangs/
121a2(mdo sde): rgyas kyi zhing gi rgyan gyi phyir smon lam yongs su dag pa ste/ drug po 'di dag go/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rgyan ni bdun po 'di dag go/ bdun gang zhe na 'di lta ste/
121a3(mdo sde): dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams la dran pa med cing / yid la byed pa med pa dang / yang dag par sreng ba rnams la skye ba med pa dang / 'gag pa med par shes pa dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams
121a4(mdo sde): kyis lus dang sems dben pa dang / dbang po rnams la dbang po yongasu shes pa dang / stobs rnams kyis bdud nyon mongs pa thams cad tshar gcod pa dang / byang chub kyi yan lag rnams
121a5(mdo sde): kyi chos thams cad kyi ngo bo nyid dang lam rnams la 'ong ba med pa dang / 'gro ba med par shes pa ste/ dngos po 'di dag go/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi shes rab
121a6(mdo sde): kyi rgyan ni brgyad po 'di dag go/ brgyad gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ shin tu zhi ba'i phyir zhi gnas shis pa dang / rab rib dang bral ba'i phyir lhag mthong shes pa dang / chos kyi phung po rjes
121a7(mdo sde): rtogs pa'i phyir phung po shes pa dang / na mkha'i khams dang mnyam pa nyid kyi phyir skye mched shes pa dang / bdag med pa'i phyir rton cing 'brel par 'byung ba shes pa dang / mi khrugs
121a8(mdo sde): pa'i phyir bden pa shes pa dang / yang dag pa ji lta bu bzhin du rab tu rtogs pas chos thams cad nges par rtogs pa shes pa ste/ brgyad po 'di dge go/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sem
121b1(mdo sde): dpa' rnams kyi shes rab kyi rgya ni dgu po 'di dag go/ dgu gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ sngon gyi mtha' dag 'das pa dang shes pa dang / phyi mi'i mtha' dag ma 'ongs pa shes pa dang / bar
121b2(mdo sde): gyi mtha' dag da ltar byung ba shes pa dang / rgyu chud mi za bas nges pa rnams sar shes dang / rkyen nye bar bsgrubs pas nges pa rnams shes pa dang / yongs su smin par byed pas/
121b3(mdo sde): logs pa nyid du nges pa rnams nges pa dang / chos kyi sku rab tu phye ba'i phyir/ sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam pa nyid du shes pa dang / 'dod chags dang bral ba'i chos kyi phyir chos thams
121b4(mdo sde): cad mnyam pa nyid du shes pa dang / 'dus ma byas kyis rab tu phye ba'i phyir/ 'phags pa thams cad mnyam pa nyid du shes pa ste/ dgu po 'di dag go// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems
121b5(mdo sde): dpa' rnams kyi shes rab kyi rgyan ni bcu po 'di dgo/ bcu gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ rnam par bsgrub pa mtshan nyid kyi phyir sgyu ma lta bur shes pa dang / yongs su brtags pa'i mtshan
121b6(mdo sde): nyid kyis phyir rmi lam lta bur shes pa dang / rnam par 'khrul pa'i mtshan nyid kyi phyir smig rgyu lta bur shes pa dang / 'pho ba med pa'i mtshan nyid kyi phyir gzugs rnyan lta bur shes
121b7(mdo sde): ba dang / 'du 'phrod kyi mtshan nyid phyir mig yor lta bur shes pa dang / rkyen gyi mtshan nyid kyi phyir brag cha lta bur shes pa dang / chos kyi dbyings 'dres pa med pa'i mtshan nyid du shes
121b8(mdo sde): ba dang / de bzhin nyid gnas pa med pa'i mtshan du shes pa dang / yang dag pa'i mtha' mi 'khrug pa'i mtshan nyid du shes pa dang / 'das byas dag 'dus byas kyi sa mtshan nyid/
122a1(mdo sde): @du shes pa ste/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi shes rab kyi rgyan ni bcu po 'di dag go/ rigs kyi bu de la byang chub sems dpa' rnams
122a2(mdo sde): gzungs kyi rgyan gang zhe na/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams gzungs kyi rgyan ni gcig go/ gcig gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ dran par byed pa med pa ste/ 'di ni gcig go// /
122a3(mdo sde): rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi gzungs kyi rgyan gnyis po 'di dag go/ gnyis gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ kun tu 'dzin pa dang 'dzin pa ste gnyis po 'di dag go// rigs kyi bu
122a4(mdo sde): byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi gzungs kyi rgyan ni gsum po 'di dag go/ gsum gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ don la mkhas pa dang / tshig 'bru la mkhas pa dang / nges pa'i tshigs la mkha
122a5(mdo sde): ba ste/ gsum po 'di dag go/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi gzungs kyi rgyan ni bzhi po 'di dag go/ bzhi gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ chags pa med pa'i tshigs dang / rtsa ba
122a6(mdo sde): ba ma yin pa'i tshigs dang / brdzun med pa'i tshig ste bzhi po 'di dag gi// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rgyan ni lnga po 'di dag go/ gang lnga gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ thos pa
122a7(mdo sde): thams cad kyi nang nas don la rtog pa dang / yi ge'i tshogs thams cad kyi nang nas ye shes la rten pa dang / mdo sde thams cad kyi nang nas nges pa'i don gyi mdo sde la ston pa dang / gang zagi smra
122a8(mdo sde): thams lnga chos nyid ston pa dang / 'jig rten thams cad la 'jig rten las 'das pa la rton pa ste/ lnga po 'di dag go// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rgyan ni drug po 'di dado//
122b1(mdo sde): drug gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ ji skad smras pa de bzhin du byed pa dang / dben pa'i rjes su 'thun pa'i tshig rab tu thob pa dang / nga rgyal med pas gzungs par 'os pa'i tshig dang g.yo med pas
122b2(mdo sde): blang bar 'os pa'i tshig dang / snying rje chen po sbyor bas 'bras bu yod pa'i chos ston pa dang / snod la mkhas pas khyad par chos ston pa dang / 'jig rten shes pas dus su chos ston pa ste/
122b3(mdo sde): drug po 'di dag go/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi gzungs kyi rgyan ni bdun po 'di dag go/ bdun gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ mgyogs pa'i spobs pa dang / shugs
122b4(mdo sde): can gyi spobs pa dang / myur ba'i spobs pa dang / chags pa med pa'i spobs pa dang / rgyun chad pa med pa'i spobs pa dang / 'khrul pa med pa'i spobs pa dang / shin tu nges
122b5(mdo sde): pa'i tshigs gis spobs pa ste/ bdun po 'di dag go// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi gzungs kyi rgyan ni brgyad po 'di dag go/ brgyad gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ lha'i skad
122b6(mdo sde): shes pa dang / klu'i skad ces pa dang / gnod sbyin gyi skad shes pa dang / dri za'i skad shes pa dang / lha ma yin gyi skad shes pa dang / nam mkha' lding gi skad shes pa dang / mi 'am
122b7(mdo sde): ci'i skad shes pa dang / lto 'phye chen po'i skad shes pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi bar gyi skad shes pa brgyad po 'di dag go// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi
122b8(mdo sde): gzungs kyi rgyan ni dgu po 'di dag go// dgu gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ 'khor gyi nang du spa gong ba med pa dang / smra ba'i nang du zhugs pa med pa dang / ches bshad pa'i nang du 'jig pa med
124a1(mdo sde): / dang 'dri ba rnams la nges par 'byung ba shes pa dang / mngon pa'i nga rgyal can rnams la snrel zhi bstan pa shes pa dang / yang dag par zhugs/
124a2(mdo sde): pa rnams la rjes su mthun pa bstan pa dang shes pa dang / khengs pa dag la lag na rdo rje ston pa dang / mngon par chags pa med pa rnams la sreg pa'i skal pa ston pa dang / yongs
124a3(mdo sde): su smin pa rnams la theg bI rim pa ji lta ba bzhin du ston pa ste/ dgu po 'di dag go// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi gzungs kyi rgyud ni bcu po 'di dag go/ bcu gang zhe na 'di
124a4(mdo sde): lta ste/ dogs pa thams cad la the tsom med pa dang / blos chos skye ba'i sgo dang / shes rab kyi snang ba gzhan la rag ma las pa dang / yi ge bstan pa mi zad pa dang / don bstan pa
124a5(mdo sde): rgyun chad pa med pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi sngags pa mtha' yas pa yang dag pa rab tu brjod pa dang / kun nas nyon mongs pa'i skyon mu med pa brjod pa dang / rnam sbyangs pa'i sngags pa
124a6(mdo sde): chad pa ba ston pa dang / dbang po thams cad la gzhol bar 'jug pa chags pa med pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi snang ba'i so so yang dag par rig pa la 'jug ga shes pa ste/ rigs kyi bu
124a7(mdo sde): byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi gzungs kyi rgyan ni bcu po de dag go/ de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis don de nyid rgya cher bstan pa'i phyir tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag gsungs so// gang
124a8(mdo sde): gis mchog dam pa 'di mdzes so// blo gros rnams kyi rgyad bzhi ste// tshul khrims ting 'dzin de bzhin shes rab mchog/ shin tu rnams nges don dang de bzhin gzungs// de ni lus
124b1(mdo sde): ca kun gyis yid 'ong dga'// lus dang ngag rnams dang ni yang dag cing // de'i rnam par ltung ba kun chad pa// 'di ni tshul khrims ldan pa'i rgyun yin na// lha mi rnams kyi nang du me khas pa
124b2(mdo sde): skye// de'i smon lam ji ltar 'dod pa bzhin du 'grub// nan tan snying por bla dang yang ldan// 'di ni tshul khrims dag pa'i rgyan yin no// de'i ting nge 'dzin sgyu ma ma yin te// shes
124b3(mdo sde): rab rnam grol de bzhin ye shes mthong // de'i mya ngan 'das pa sgyu ma min// 'di ni tshul khrims rnam par dag pa'i rgyan// tshul khrims skyon med tshul khrims rnam par dag/ tshul
124b4(mdo sde): khrims 'thun chags ma yin 'dren med// de'i rangs dga' de bzhengs rarangs dbang yin// 'di ni tshul khrims pang dag pa'i rgyan// tshul khrims kyis ni sbyin pa dag par 'gyur/
124b5(mdo sde): bzod pa dag cing de bzhin brtson 'grus dag/ bsam gtan dag cing de bzhin shes rab dag/ thabs dang de bzhin bag yod dag yin// g.yo ba med cing brtan la shin du gnas// /
124b6(mdo sde): sa mchog thob cing rnal 'byor rnam 'phro med// lhod pa spangs shing dgang sla gso yang sla// 'di ni gang dag tshul khrims dag pa'i rgyan// brtson 'grus 'bar zhing tshul khrims
124b7(mdo sde): bsngags pa ste// de'i sems ni nam yang gdung mi 'gyur// de la yid la gcags par 'gyur med de// 'di ni gang dag tshul khrims dag pa'i rgyan// 'jigs pa med cing mi skra
124b8(mdo sde): mi zhum ste// bsam pa nges shing zhi la yid rab zhi// 'dir ni de'i bcings pa lhod par 'gyur// 'di ni gang dag tshul khrims dag pa'i rgyan// grags chen sems ni las su rung
125a1(mdo sde): ba yin// de ni dul zhing de bzhin cing shes yin// 'dir ni rang lus mtshan gyi brgyan byed pa// 'di ni gang dag tshul khrims dag pa'i rgyan// de ni ji skad smras
125a2(mdo sde): pa de bzhin byed// mkhas pa de ni ngag gi rgyan thob ste/ de ni nyon mongs pa med pas rtags sems rgyan// 'di ni gang dag tshul khrims dag pa'i rgyan// khyed par 'phags pa'i
125a3(mdo sde): zhing ni legs par rgyan// theg pa mchog la sems can yongs smin byed// gang phyin sdig thams cad mi byed pas// rang gi skye ba legs par brgyan par byed// byang chub spyod pa rtag
125a4(mdo sde): tu brgyan byed cing // byang chub snying po dam pa rgyan par byed// stobs dang mi 'jigs pa dag rgyan byed cing // nga rgyal med pas shes pa legs par brgyan// de ni byams pas
125a5(mdo sde): sems can kun khyab ste// mkhas pa rtag tu drang dang mnyen pa yin// g.yo ba med cing sgyu med bcos med// gti mug 'dod dang 'jigs pas 'gro ma yin// de ni sgri pa
125a6(mdo sde): lnga po rnam par sel// bag yod gyur nas rjes su dran drug bsgom// byang chub yan lag bdun dang lam bsgom ste// mthar gyi sa dgu dang ting 'dzin bsam gtan byed// rnal 'byor
125a7(mdo sde): ba ni gzhi gnas nges sems sbyor// de ni tshul bzhin dge ba rlud mi bzod// dben dang shin tu sbyangs dang so sor rtog/ 'phags pa'i rigs la dbang ni sbyar ba yin// chos
125a8(mdo sde): rnams ni the tsom med par 'gyur// de la kun nas ldang dang 'gyur ba med// de la ma rig gti mug mun pa med// bden pa snang zhing yongs su shes pa shes// tshul khrims dag
125b1(mdo sde): pa dmigs pa med pa ste// shes rab dam pa bsam gtan ting 'dzin dag/ gnyis bsal nas ni rnam par dgrol ba dgalhag pa'i nga rgyal med cing shes pa dang // dus
125b2(mdo sde): sum dag la ye shes mthong mi chags// 'dod chags bral ba'i shes pas chos kyang dag/ dag nas 'dir ni de la rloms sems med// 'di ni shang dag shes rab ldan pa'i rgyan//
125b3(mdo sde): shes rab kyis ni sbyin pa rgyan gyur te// rmi lam sgyu ma tshol ba med pa'i phyir// bdag dang byang chub de bzhin sems rnams// 'khor gsum de dag de ni rnam par sbyong // /
125b4(mdo sde): shes rab kyi ni tshul khrims brgyan gyur te// gzugs brnyan sgyu ma brag cha 'dra ba'i phyir/ lus dang ngag rnams dang ni de bzhin sems// 'khor gsum po dag de ni rnam
125b5(mdo sde): bar spong // shes rab kyis ni bzod pa'i rgyan gyur te// khams dang mtho ba ma yin dma' bar 'gyur min dang // dam pa'i chos kun rtag tu rab rtog pa// 'khor gsum po
125b6(mdo sde): dag de ni rnam par spong // shes rab kyis ni rtson 'grus rgyan gyur te// sko ba med cing bsam gtan pa dang // de ni blang ba med cing der med pa// 'khor gsum po dag
125b7(mdo sde): de ni rnam par dag spyod// shes rab kyis ni bsam gtan rgyan gyur te// de ma chags gyur dang lhag mthong dang // mkhas pa mngon par shes pa skyed pa dang // 'khor ga suM
125b8(mdo sde): po dag de ni rnam par sbyong // shes rab kyis ni thabs dang rgyan byed de// shin tu sdu ba gzugs dang yang dag smon// 'khor gsum po dag de ni rnam par sbyong zhing // sems
127a1(mdo sde): can chos dang de bzhin zhing rnams sbyong // dran pa nye bar bzhag la dran mi 'jug/ yang dag bong ba la gnyis med de// rdzu 'phrul gyis ni lus dang sems
127a2(mdo sde): kyang dben// sems can gyis ni dbang po kun mi shes// bdud dang nyon mongs rnams kyis zil mi non// chos kyi rang bzhin tshul bzhin rjes su rtogs// de bzhin lam la 'ong med 'gro
127a3(mdo sde): ba med// 'di ni gang dag shes rab ldan pa'i rgyan// de ni shin tu zhi ba sa gzhi gnas shes pa// de'i lhag mthong spyod yul mtha' yas te// chos kyi phung po shes pa phung po bzhin// /
127a4(mdo sde): khams ni nam mkha' mtshungs shing 'dra bar shes// des ni stong pa lta bur skye mched shes// rten pas bsags pas chos rnams bdag med de// don dam dben par 'khrug pa
127a5(mdo sde): shes// tshul bzhin gyis ni nges par rtog par shes// dus gsum la ni tshogs med 'jug/ rnam par gzhag phyir phung po gsum yang shes// dkon mchog gsum ni mtshan

127a7(mdo sde): rgyu 'dra ba ste// 'pho med chos rnams gzugs rnyen mtshan nyid do// 'du 'phro byung ba mig yer lta bu ste// rkyen rnams kyis na brag cha ji bzhin no// chos kyi dbyings ni rtag tu ma 'dres shes/
127a8(mdo sde): de bzhin nyid ni gnas med de rab shes// yang dag mtha' ni rtag tu mi g.yo chos// 'dus ma byas dang 'dus byas gnyis su med// shes rab zab cing blo ni rab yangs pa/ brgyad
127b1(mdo sde): nas sangs rgyas chos rnams tshol bar byed// de ni nam yang dran pa brjed pa med// chos rnams kun tu 'dzin cing 'dzin par byed// don dang tshig 'bru la ni rtag tu mkhas//
127b2(mdo sde): nges tshigs shes pa rtag par rtogs khong chud// chags med tshig dang rtsa ba ma yin dang // rab tu grol ba'i tshig dang brdzun med tshig/ chos pa kun don rtag tu rtog pa dang //

163b2(mdo sde): the tsom gyi rgyu las skye ba yang yod de/ de dag kyang de bzhin gshegs pas rab tu shes so// rigs kyi bu gzhan yang dbang po rno ba'i phyir/ rka bi'i lam la mngon par shes pa rgyur
163b3(mdo sde): pa yang de bzhin go shegs pas rab tu shes so// dbang po rtul ba'i lam la mngon par shes pa la bul ba yang rab tu shes so// dbang po rnon po'i phyir sla ba'i phyir lam la mngon
163b4(mdo sde): par shes pa myur ba yang rab tu shes so// dbang po rno ba'i phyir sla ba'i lam la mngon par shes so// dbang po rtul ba'i phyir sla ba'i lam la mngon par shes pa bul ba yang rab tu

163b6(mdo sde): rab tu shes so// yongs su thug pa med par dbugs 'byin pa'i phyir/ myur ba'i lam la mngon par shes pa bul ba yang rab tu shes so// so sor rtog pa'i stobs yongasu
163b7(mdo sde): rdzogs par byed kyi/ sgom pa'i stobs lam ma yin pa'i lam yang yod de// de'ang de bzhin gshegs pas rab tu shes so// sgom pa'i stobs yongs su rdzogs par byed kyi/
163b8(mdo sde): so sor rtog pa'i stobs lam yin pa'i lam yang yod de de'ang de bzhin gshegs pas rab tu shes so// so sor rtog pa'i stobs kyang yongs su rdzogs par mi byed la/ sgom pa'i
164a1(mdo sde): stobs la yang ma yin pa'i lam yang yod de de yang de bzhin gshegs pas rab tu shes so// so sor rtog pa'i stobs dang / sgom pa'i stobs kyang yongs su
164a2(mdo sde): rdzogs par byed pa'i lam yang yod de de'ang de bzhin gshegs pas rab tu shes so// bsam pa phun sum 'tshegs pa la sbyor ba phun sum tshogs pa ma yin pa'i lam yang yod
164a3(mdo sde): de de bzhin gshegs pas rab tu shes so// sbyor ba phun sum 'tshogs pa la/ bsam pa phun sum 'tshogs pa ma yin pa'i lam yang yod de de'ang de bzhin gshegs pas rab tu sheso// /
164a4(mdo sde): bsam pa yang phun sum 'tshogs pa ma yin la sbyor ba phun sum 'tshogs pa ma yin pa'i lam yang yod/ bsame pa phun sum tshogs la/ sbyor ba'ang phun sum tshogs pa'i lam

164a6(mdo sde): yin pa'i lam yang yod/ lus dang ngag dang sems kyang sbyor ba'i lam yang yod/ lus ma yin pa gang yang ma yin la/ sems la ma yin pa'i lam yang yod/ lus dang

164b1(mdo sde): bzhin gshegs pa'i las drug pa'o// de la 'di skad ces bya'o// bde bar gshegs pas lam kun rab shes shing ngas dang rgyu bcas pa'i sems can khams kyang shes/ ma nges
164b2(mdo sde): yongs su smin par bya ba'i mtshan nyid dang ni de bzhin snod min log par lta ldan dang // 'dod chags rnam sum lam ldan dag dang / zhe sdang rnam pa gsum dang de bzhin gti mug ldan pa dang //

165a1(mdo sde): lus dang sems kyang sbyong bar byed pa'i lam dang ji ltar 'jug par 'gyur dang ldog pa dang / ye shes ni sems gzigs pas ye shes 'di yang bde bar gshegs kyi

165a4(mdo sde): rkyen gang yin pa de'ang de bzhin gshegs pas rab tu shes so// de la rgyu ni gang rkyen na gang zhe na/ sems can rnam rnam par dag par 'gyur ba'i rgyu gang yin pa dang / rkyen gang yin pa de

165a6(mdo sde): kyi rkyen ni ma rig pa'o// ma rig pa ni rgyu'o 'du byed rnams ni rkyen to// 'du byed ni rgyu'o// rnam par shes pa ni rkyen to rnam par shes pa ni rgyu'o// ming dang gzugs ni rkyen to// ming dang

167a1(mdo sde): / dang rgyu lasu kun tu 'byeng ba de 'di rkyen// 'gro ba rnam dag 'gyur ba'i rgyu dang rkyen ni gnyis po// gzhan las mthun pa'i sgra thos pa dang / thos nas kyang chos rnams
